 บ    Reporter : Rebel Chicken             Interviewee : The Speed Racer      บ
 บ    Subject  : The #1 Games Group?       Affiliation : Razor 1911 Leader    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: How do you think Razor (Razor 1911) currently rates against other   บ
 บ        games groups in the scene?  Razor has been the #1 games group in    บ
 บ        the scene for many years now, but do you believe that it is still   บ
 บ        the #1 games group?                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RZR: I think that Razor will always be the #1 games group due to the     บ
 บ        fact that every game we release is quality and we pretest our       บ
 บ        games so that the end user will not have wasted his time            บ
 บ        downloading a non-working game.  Also bear in mind that although    บ
 บ        Razor may not be the #1 games group in the games chart, we are      บ
 บ        consistent.  I personally have seen many groups come and go in the  บ
 บ        past two years, some dynasties like Pentagram, TDU-Jam, and         บ
 บ        Hybrid.  Hybrid is back though after it had died earlier when it    บ
 บ        tried merging into another games group known as Dynamix which is    บ
 บ        also dead now.  But as these many groups come and go, in the end,   บ
 บ        there can only be one Razor!                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: True, Razor will always be around even when other groups come and   บ
 บ        go.  I've been downloading Razor games since late 1994.  I          บ
 บ        remember sometime in 1994 that I found a text being spread saying   บ
 บ        that Razor had officially disbanded.  I was in shock because all    บ
 บ        of my friends had told me that Razor was a legendary group that     บ
 บ        would be around indefinitely.  I read the text file on Razor        บ
 บ        1911's death, and I found out that TRC (The Renegade Chemist) who   บ
 บ        who was a Razor leader at the time, decided to disband Razor.  He   บ
 บ        claimed that he had disagreements with many other Razor members.    บ
 บ        A few weeks later, I was surprised to see that Razor did not die,   บ
 บ        and that you were the new leader.  How did you become the leader    บ
 บ        of Razor 1911?  It is ironic to see that TRC is now a leader of     บ
 บ        Prestige, Razor's closest competitor.                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RZR: In December of 1994, TRC had wanted to close down Razor saying      บ
 บ        that it was the best floppy game releasing group of all time and    บ
 บ        that the group should not continue due to the fact of the           บ
 บ        diminishing amount of floppy game releases.                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: That's stupid of TRC, right after he disbanded Razor, didn't he go  บ
 บ        on to start his new floppy games group called Eclipse?  What was    บ
 บ        he smoking?                                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RZR: I took it upon myself to get a general consensus of the group, and  บ
 บ        I found that the majority did not want the group killed.            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Of course not, Razor has always been a dominant force in the        บ
 บ        scene, it would be absurd to kill such a good group.                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RZR: With the backing of The Gecko and EOS, I called up the Razor        บ
 บ        distribution sites and suppliers and rallied them around.  At that  บ
 บ        point, TRC was surprised to see such a gathering and put up a       บ
 บ        fight with Marauder siding with TRC and Randall Flagg helping.      บ
 บ        The text file being spread was actually a private message that TRC  บ
 บ        wrote in the Razor Conference on The Assassin's Guild, which was    บ
 บ        the Razor WHQ at the time.  King Lear, a Razor courier, took the    บ
 บ        private message and spread it as a text file, he was booted out of  บ
 บ        Razor for doing it.  After about a month, Marauder was the one      บ
 บ        supplier that supplied a few games with his razor.nfo which had     บ
 บ        TRC listed in it.  The rest of the suppliers were using my          บ
 บ        razor.nfo which did not include TRC.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: So there were TWO razor.nfos?                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RZR: The final showdown would come on The Assassin's Guild when TRC was  บ
 บ        pumping up his version of Rise of the Triad and the rest of Razor   บ
 บ        pumped up my version with my nfo.  Imagine that two Razor releases  บ
 บ        of the same game with different razor.nfos were being pumped up in  บ
 บ        a race, what a rush!                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Yup, what a rush.                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RZR: After seeing his loss on The Ghetto, which later becomes the        บ
 บ        Eclipse WHQ, TRC gracefully admitted his loss and that he was no    บ
 บ        longer in Razor.  After that, we turned around our attention and    บ
 บ        we started a mad releasing frenzy.  TRC was filled with revenge     บ
 บ        and hatred and after claiming he would retire, he then started      บ
 บ        Eclipse which would die three months later, then he jumped to       บ
 บ        Hybrid which would die four months later, then he went to Dynamix   บ
 บ        which lasted four months, and now he is finally with Prestige, a    บ
 บ        currently good games releasing group.                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Why did you have this race with TRC in the first place?  Why were   บ
 บ        there two separate razor.nfos, one with TRC in it, and one          บ
 บ        without?  How could this have happened?                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RZR: In my razor.nfo, TRC was not listed cause we had kicked him out so  บ
 บ        he was trying to out release us with his name in his nfo to show    บ
 บ        that he had power in the group.                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: What an idiot!  If you're not wanted in a group, you might as well  บ
 บ        leave it.  Was TRC hard to work with?  Why did he have to show      บ
 บ        that he had power in the group?  Is he some kind of power hungry    บ
 บ        punk?  Last time I chatted with him, he said to me, "But I am       บ
 บ        god!"  And when I did not acknowledge the fact that he was a god,   บ
 บ        he got really really mad at me.                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RZR: TRC is very knowledgeable in supplying games, but he is very        บ
 บ        arrogant and cocky when it comes to dealing with people which       บ
 บ        usually rubs people the wrong way.                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: How is he knowledgeable in supplying?  What does he do that no one  บ
 บ        else can?  I'm sure he does not work for a games company, they      บ
 บ        wouldn't hire someone like him.  How does he supply?  I'm sure TRC  บ
 บ        doesn't supply games by doing store pick up because he always       บ
 บ        makes fun of Pest from Razor for doing that.                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RZR: TRC uses various methods and he does do store pick up and evidence  บ
 บ        of that would be his release of the game "Hoyles Solitaire."        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Yeah, Prestige released Hoyles Solitaire the same day it shipped    บ
 บ        into my store.  I work for Egghead, so I know these things.         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RZR: If you would've been on top of your game you could have beaten      บ
 บ        him.                                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Thanks but no thanks.  I don't supply.  I like to keep myself       บ
 บ        clean for purposes of being an RCN editor.  And I think supplying   บ
 บ        is a bore, don't take it the wrong way, it's just my personal bias  บ
 บ        toward taking games home, ripping them, cracking them, testing      บ
 บ        them, packaging them, and then uploading them to some board for     บ
 บ        credits.  There are already enough people who can do that.  Did     บ
 บ        TRC pose problems for Razor even after he left it?  Has he done     บ
 บ        anything that would hinder Razor's work ethics, or its release      บ
 บ        potential?                                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RZR: TRC has tried to kill the group or damage it by trying to steal     บ
 บ        some former HQs which supplied games and other suppliers as well,   บ
 บ        but people in general like working with me which is why they have   บ
 บ        stayed loyal to me and the group.                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Of course, nobody likes to work with someone that has a fucking     บ
 บ        napaoleon complex, but either way, when you found out that TRC was  บ
 บ        trying to kill Razor and was trying to steal Razor suppliers, how   บ
 บ        did you react?  Did you try to stop him?                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RZR: Luckily, I have great informers and everyone is loyal to me so I    บ
 บ        managed to secure everything.  Except for maybe a few traders that  บ
 บ        left Razor, he got away with nothing.                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: You said earlier that Eclipse lasted four months with TRC running   บ
 บ        it, and you then mentioned that Hybrid and Dynamix also only        บ
 บ        lasted four months.  Do you belive perhaps that Prestige would not  บ
 บ        last much longer than four months also, since it's being run by     บ
 บ        TRC?                                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RZR: TRC is from what I am led to believe a minor leader, Zion and       บ
 บ        Speed Master are the leaders with Shadow Master also advising.      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Yeah right, tell TRC that he is only a minor leader in Prestige     บ
 บ        and he'll blow up.  You also mentioned earlier that the reason why  บ
 บ        Razor is the #1 games group is because it consistenly releases      บ
 บ        good quality games that are tested to make sure that they work, do  บ
 บ        you believe that there are other games groups out there that might  บ
 บ        also match Razor's quality?                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RZR: For now and the MOST part Prestige and Hybrid do release quality    บ
 บ        working games, and I hope they continue doing a good job doing so   บ
 บ        because in the end, the whole scene benefits from a good release.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Yes, and that's a great attitude toward your competitors.           บ

 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: What is your current position in Legion?  And what were your        บ
 บ        duties for the group?                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ AOD: I was a net coordinator before Acidplain had cut me for no reason,  บ
 บ        and what I basically did was upload to Oasis and BBX for Legion     บ
 บ        and help out couriers.                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Acidplain just decided to cut your position as a net coordinator    บ
 บ        for Legion for absolutely NO reason?  I'm sure Acidplain must have  บ
 บ        been ticked off about something right?  He wouldn't have just gone  บ
 บ        around cutting members from Legion without a valid cause.  Were     บ
 บ        there any happenings prior to him cutting you from the group?       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ AOD: It started about 6 months ago when the courier group Digital was    บ
 บ        still active in the scene.  Acidplain was accepted into Digital as  บ
 บ        a member by Devast, a Digital Leader.  Acidplain told Devast that   บ
 บ        he could get Digital t3 sites, but it turned out that Acidplain     บ
 บ        lied to Devast and when Devast found out, Devast kicked Acidplain   บ
 บ        out of the group.  This morning, X-Factor, a co-leader of Legion,   บ
 บ        was angry with Acidplain because he hasn't done one good thing for  บ
 บ        Legion.  I agreed with X-Factor on that note and also told him      บ
 บ        about Acidplain's prior reputation as a Digital member.  Acidplain  บ
 บ        must have overheard what had happened and since he always hated     บ
 บ        me, he cut me.                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: When you say that he cut you, you are referring to him kicking you  บ
 บ        out of the group right?  Were any other members cut as a result of  บ
 บ        what you said?                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ AOD: Yes, when I was still a net coordinator, X-Factor had told me to    บ
 บ        help him make a few cuts.  When I came up with the list, Acidplain  บ
 บ        said that I too was cut from the group.                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Do you believe that perhaps Acidplain might be doing more good for  บ
 บ        Legion if he left?  After all, it seems to me that he might only    บ
 บ        be atrophying Legion's already tarred reputation.                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ AOD: First of all, I would like to get one thing straight, I do not      บ
 บ        consider Acidplain leet at all, many people will agree with me on   บ
 บ        this.  He has done nothing for the group so far and even his        บ
 บ        co-leaders agree.  I must admit that his co-leaders are doing a     บ
 บ        really good job though.  I could tell you that if he were to leave  บ
 บ        Legion, there would be no tears shed by anyone, in other words, he  บ
 บ        wouldn't make the group any worse.                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Perhaps he does serve a purpose that benefits the group, but it     บ
 บ        just so happens that nobody can see what he does for the group?     บ
 บ        After all, if he did nothing for Legion, wouldn't he be kicked out  บ
 บ        of the group by now, or perhaps he will be kicked out soon?         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ AOD: No, I don't think he'll get kicked out because the co-leaders       บ
 บ        don't want to do it because they are scared to.  But I can tell     บ
 บ        you for a fact that one of the co-leaders has been thinking about   บ
 บ        it.                                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: How many co-leaders are there in Legion?  If there aren't more      บ
 บ        than 3 leaders in Legion, then that should really narrow it down    บ
 บ        to who has been thinking of kicking Acidplain out of Legion.        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ AOD: Well, there are 3 leaders currently, but I think Acidplain was the  บ
 บ        founder although he doesn't do *NEARLY* as much as any of the       บ
 บ        other leaders.                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: He might not be doing much good for Legion, but we all know that    บ
 บ        Acidplain is doing SOMETHING for Legion.  After all, we all know    บ
 บ        that he's been out doing stupid things like starting wars with      บ
 บ        more popular utils groups such as Pinnacle.  There is even          บ
 บ        evidence that he has been trying to steal suppliers from Pinnacle   บ
 บ        for Legion.  Acidplain has also been caught flooding channel        บ
 บ        #Pinnacle like he was a 12 year old dickless lamer.  Do the Legion  บ
 บ        leaders and members stand behind his actions?                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ AOD: Well, many Legion members are afraid to stand up against Acidplain  บ
 บ        because they all know that he is very immature.  If you speak out   บ
 บ        against him, you get cut from Legion like that.  And yes, I         บ
 บ        believe that he has been stealing suppliers from other utils        บ
 บ        groups.  I don't know whether he has stopped flooding channel       บ
 บ        #Pinnacle though.                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: How old is Acidplain?                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ AOD: Well, I don't know how old he is, but when I asked him how old he   บ
 บ        was, he replied, "How old is your mom?"  That alone should give     บ
 บ        you a picture of how immature he is.  Legion is still a good utils  บ
 บ        group, it's just that things would be a lot more peaceful without   บ
 บ        a wannabe like Acidplain running around.                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ

 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Reporter : Zima Man                  Interviewee : Zoltrix              บ
 บ    Subject  : PCWarez                   Affiliation : PCW President        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Please tell us who you are and what you do.                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ PCW: I am the founder of PCWarez.                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: What kind of group is PCW and what is it's specialty?               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ PCW: Well, PCWarez is a release group specializing mainly in utilities   บ
 บ        and once in a while the odd game and cd-rip.                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: How old is PCW and how was it founded?                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ PCW: PCW was founded in February of 1996.  We're going on our 1/2 year   บ
 บ        anniversary.  And basically it was a few of us that got anooyed     บ
 บ        listening to other groups nagging at us so we started our own       บ
 บ        small group that has now grown to +90 hard working mambers.         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: You have more then 90 members?  That's quite a lot, please tell us  บ
 บ        why your group size is so big?                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ PCW: Well, we have our own couriers within the group as well as courier  บ
 บ        groups, we figure the more people the more the warez will get       บ
 บ        around.                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: So your group is very strong courier wise, where do you spread you  บ
 บ        files first on BBS's or FTP's?                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ PCW: Well, I would say it is sent to both equally because we have split  บ
 บ        the couriers in 2 groups, Internet and BBS so they get the files    บ
 บ        to both pretty much at the same time, as well as we have PTA        บ
 บ        (Power Trading Arsenal) offering on IRC and couriering to FTP as    บ
 บ        well.                                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: You said before that your group is a uni-releasing group, how come  บ
 บ        you don't concentrate on only utils or games?                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ PCW: Well we try to stay mostly with utils but if the game is cool and   บ
 บ        we have it handy then why not?                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: What is your source of getting releases?                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ PCW: Well, we have a few ways, we have suppliers who buy or rent the     บ
 บ        programs, as well as a few suppliers employed in companies wich     บ
 บ        provide software.                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: What do you mean rent programs?  Where I come from, there are no    บ
 บ        programs available for rent, the only source is either to buy them  บ
 บ        or pirate them!                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ PCW: Well, here in Canada there are stores wich rent out cds and         บ
 บ        software, who knows if it is legal or not but they do it!!  And     บ
 บ        these are reputable stores.  We even have certain video stores      บ
 บ        which rent out games.                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: PCW was never a big releasing group, but in the last few weeks you  บ
 บ        have released quite a lot of programs.  How many releases do you    บ
 บ        put out in an average week?                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ PCW: It varies every week!  Sometimes we have nothing and sometimes we   บ
 บ        can release up to 7 to 8 releases a week, but we are still fairly   บ
 บ        young I would like to eventually have it to at least 10 releases a  บ
 บ        week every week.                                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: There was a rumour that one of PCW suppliers had Quake Final Beta   บ
 บ        before it was released by ROR but for some strange reason, you      บ
 บ        didn't release.  Why did you pass on on such a great game?          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ PCW: Yes, that is true we had a supplier that had the beta but spent     บ
 บ        all day and night playing the game that we missed the chance and    บ
 บ        ROR released it.  We were not seriously concerned with it anyways   บ
 บ        as we try to stay mostly with the utils.                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: When you spread your files, to which FTPs and BBSes do they go      บ
 บ        first?                                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ PCW: Well, we have all the releases sent to our FTPs and our BBSes       บ
 บ        first and from there the couriers take them to the rest of the      บ
 บ        sites and boards I could not name all the places they go there are  บ
 บ        so many couriers I would never be able to keep track of that all I  บ
 บ        care is that they get out to people.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Many groups usually upload to big FTPs and BBSes in order not to    บ
 บ        be beaten by other groups, how come you don't do the same?          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ PCW: Like I said, my main concern is getting the files out to the        บ
 บ        people, I like to think we have couriers getting them to the big    บ
 บ        sites first seeing as we give them the files first, but as long as  บ
 บ        they get out and spread quickly.                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: How worldwide spread is PCW?                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ PCW: Well, we cover mostly Canada and United States, but we also have    บ
 บ        people in Europe, Russia, South America, and Middle East so I       บ
 บ        would say we are pretty well covered.                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: What are the future plans for PCW?                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ PCW: Well, our future goal is to be up there along side Razor, PWA and   บ
 บ        the other big groups but for the near future we would just like to  บ
 บ        release a lot more warez for the people to enjoy!                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ RCN: Ok, thanks a lot for the interview and is there anything you want   บ
 บ        to say in the closing?                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ PCW: Yes, I would just like to say for everyone to keep an eye out for   บ
 บ        PCWAREZ and enjoy our releases!  Also, to all you group             บ
 บ        prezidents, watch out for Acidplain, he enjoys sneaking in your     บ
 บ        group and stealing your members while you are not looking... very   บ
 บ        lame!                                                               บ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Hitex                                                         บ
 บ    Subject : Describing Your Releases                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Recently the scene has seen more releases per day than at any other   บ
 บ  time.  A great contributor to this are the software companies             บ
 บ  themselves.  Just as new groups pop up every day, new software companies  บ
 บ  pop up every day.  And just as most new groups are complete fluff, and    บ
 บ  release nothing but crap, most new software companies are the same way.   บ
 บ  They care more about getting releases out the door quickly than they do   บ
 บ  about taking the time to properly program them.  In fact -- and yes, I'm  บ
 บ  still talking about the companies here -- sometimes they don't even do a  บ
 บ  proper job of packaging their releases!  I remember back in my Legacy     บ
 บ  (LGC) days, we had a release called "Nemesis II" that didn't work right   บ
 บ  off the CD!  We contacted the company and apparently they had forgotten   บ
 บ  to place a file crucial for play under Windows 95 on the CD.  It makes    บ
 บ  you wonder if they ever beta test their releases.  What's worse is that   บ
 บ  the companies are sinking to the level of the piraters they are trying    บ
 บ  to eliminate!                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      As soon as a company releases one of these                            บ
 บ  bad/lame/stupid/low-quality releases, the scene does as well, and that's  บ
 บ  to be expected, but many people in the scene don't want to download       บ
 บ  these releases because they are exactly that, low in quality.  That's     บ
 บ  where the problem WE can control comes into play.  I can't blame a group  บ
 บ  for releasing this kind of crap, the scene is one big competition, and    บ
 บ  it is definitely a legitimate way of trying to climb up in the release    บ
 บ  scale, but it's not right when the releasing groups label the release     บ
 บ  with a wonderful tag.  Let's say a company just released "Flight for      บ
 บ  Fun! for Windows 95."  Sounds like a dandy release to me, but the group   บ
 บ  gets it and notices it's complete crap.  Then, their NFO rates the        บ
 บ  release "[ooooooooo.] [09/10]."  A look down will yield release           บ
 บ  information stating that the program is "A kick-ass flight simulator."    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      In these competitive times, I don't blame groups for releasing        บ
 บ  anything and everything that they get their hands on, but there is no     บ
 บ  excuse for this sort of behavior.  There are two main items that can      บ
 บ  always be expected in releases in the scene today.  They are A) A         บ
 บ  FILE_ID.DIZ file so that when the file is uploaded to a BBS, it will      บ
 บ  automatically extrapolate the description, and B) a group NFO file so     บ
 บ  that the end users can find out information about the releasing group,    บ
 บ  and so that they can find out about the program they might want to        บ
 บ  download.  Good practice would be to fill the release info section of     บ
 บ  the release with the text on the back of the box, that should give the    บ
 บ  end user enough information about what the release is, and then a short   บ
 บ  few lines about the group's assessment of the program.  If it says that   บ
 บ  it recommends a 486 DX 33 MHz and the group ran it on a Pentium 100 and   บ
 บ  the scrolling was unbearably slow, mention that the release might only    บ
 บ  be ideal on a Pentium of at least 133 MHz.  If the group is lazy          บ
 บ  (laziness will never get you to the top) just a bit of information found  บ
 บ  out while testing the program could suffice.                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      What is NOT acceptable is when a group puts in 1 line of text about   บ
 บ  the program that any idiot could infer from the program name found in     บ
 บ  the DIZ (though don't take that for granted, a group recently forgot to   บ
 บ  put the name of the program in their DIZ).  What's worse is when a        บ
 บ  respected group does this.  I will offer you some examples.               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Convert Plus - Released by DOD                                            บ
 บ  ฺฤฤออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออฤฤฟ  บ
 บ  ณ Just unzip the files in to "disk" dirs' and install it.              ณ  บ
 บ  ณ                                                              -AZZ-   ณ  บ
 บ  รฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤด  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I took a gamble when I downloaded this program because I didn't know  บ
 บ  exactly WHAT it would convert, fortunately I won, this is a WONDERFUL     บ
 บ  release by DOD, unfortunately many probably passed this one up due to     บ
 บ  DOD's skimpy description.  A more appropriate description would have      บ
 บ  been :                                                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      "A wonderful program that will let you convert between all kinds of   บ
 บ  formats such as Word Processing, Database, Graphics, and Spreadsheet      บ
 บ  formats quite quickly and very well.  In fact, this program will even     บ
 บ  let you read Macintosh floppy disks (it even works on iOMEGA ZIP disks!)  บ
 บ  and will add seamless Macintosh media support to your Windows 95          บ
 บ  interface!  A must get for any person that would ever have to do          บ
 บ  cross-platform work!  To install merely unzip the files in to 'disk'      บ
 บ  dirs' and install it."                                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ   pcAnywhere for Windows 95 - Released by PWA                              บ
 บ  ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป  บ
 บ  บ [pcAnywhere 7.5 32bit        ]  Released at [14:20:00] on [ 6/29/96 ]บ  บ
 บ  วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ  บ
 บ  บ Supplier .....:Wired            ณ Type .....:Remote Control          บ  บ
 บ  บ Cracker ......:N/A              ณ Video ....:yup                     บ  บ
 บ  บ Packager .....:Mercy            ณ Audio ....:nope                    บ  บ
 บ  บ Protection ...:N/A              ณ Rating ...: []           บ  บ
 บ  ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ  บ
 บ   To install unzip each file into a dir named disk1, disk2, disk3, disk4   บ
 บ   and run setup...                                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      What makes PWA think that just because this is a popular program,     บ
 บ  they don't have to describe it?  The most you can infer from the PWA NFO  บ
 บ  comes out of their "Type" field, suggesting it is a "Remote Control"      บ
 บ  program.  However, that would mean, to your average user, that it is a    บ
 บ  program for infra-red control of your computer, or something to that      บ
 บ  nature.  If a group has the balls to rate one of their releases 10/10,    บ
 บ  as PWA did with this release, it should at least say a few words to back  บ
 บ  that up!  A more appropriate description would have been :                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      "A remote access program for accessing your PC from other locations   บ
 บ  via a modem.  You get file transfer features as well as printer control   บ
 บ  features, a great program to have if you need to access programs from     บ
 บ  your work PC from your home, and don't feel like traveling back to work   บ
 บ  to get them."                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ   Gender Wars - Released by Razor 1911                                     บ
 บ  ณ                            Game Notes                               ณ   บ
 บ  ณ                           ~~~~~~~~~~~~                              ณ   บ
 บ  ณ  Razor 1911 proudly presents Gender Wars (c) GT Intgeractive.       ณ   บ
 บ  ณ  This is an action/strategy type game, which features crisp game    ณ   บ
 บ  ณ  GFX, and exploding sound effects.  Choose you SEX, cuz the battle  ณ   บ
 บ  ณ  is on.  Enjoy this title from the one and only RAZOR 1911.         ณ   บ
 บ  ณ                                                                     ณ   บ
 บ  ณ                        Installation Guide                           ณ   บ
 บ  ณ                       ~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~                          ณ   บ
 บ  ณ  In order for this game to run properly, you MUST substitute X:     ณ   บ
 บ  ณ  for ?:\GENDER in order for this game to work.  We appologize for   ณ   บ
 บ  ณ  any inconvenience this may cause you, but it is the only way we    ณ   บ
 บ  ณ  can get this game to work.  It is worth it though.  Once you have  ณ   บ
 บ  ณ  substituted, run INSTALL, and follow the prompts.  Be sure NOT to  ณ   บ
 บ  ณ  to delete the entirety of the installation directory, keep the     ณ   บ
 บ  ณ  Subdirectories within, they are required.  Once done, copy the     ณ   บ
 บ  ณ  GW.EXE supplied in installation dir to the C:\GW, and play.        ณ   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Now THAT is an example of a great NFO.  Adequate description of the   บ
 บ  game, and ample information about how to install it.  I admit that        บ
 บ  install utils is easier than installing games, but I've seen too many     บ
 บ  games released with the same amount of data as the above utils.  Razor    บ
 บ  did a great job here, and their NFO shows that they took time in finding  บ
 บ  the easiest way to install the program, pointing out that "we apologize   บ
 บ  for any inconvenience this may cause you, but it is the only way we can   บ
 บ  get this game to work." (speaking of the SUBST installation procedure)    บ
 บ  Great work by Razor 1911, but does this really seem so hard?  PWA or DOD  บ
 บ  could have just as easily taken another minute to properly describe       บ
 บ  their releases.                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I'm sure that I've passed up many great releases merely because the   บ
 บ  groups that released them didn't take that extra minute to let us know    บ
 บ  what it is that they just released.  I have much greater respect for the  บ
 บ  group whose releases I have yet to download because the descriptions      บ
 บ  never interested me, than the group whose releases I always download,     บ
 บ  just to find that I wasted my time as a result of them not taking the     บ
 บ  time to tell me what they released.                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Rebel Chicken                                                 บ
 บ    Subject : Prophet of Napalm, BUSTED!                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A few weeks ago, Napalm released Battle Arena Toshinden a few         บ
 บ  minutes after Prestige released the same game.  Surprisingly, both        บ
 บ  groups released identical cracks for the game which would lead one to     บ
 บ  believe that one group must have stolen the crack from the other.         บ
 บ  Prestige accused Prophet, a Napalm Leader, of stealing the crack, but     บ
 บ  Prophet had a good enough reputation in the scene not to fall easily to   บ
 บ  such atrocious accusations.  Even though Prestige had enough evidence to  บ
 บ  show that Prophet did indeed steal the crack for Battle Arena Toshinden,  บ
 บ  the general concesus was that Prophet would not have stooped so low.      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Once again, Prophet is accused of stealing.  However, this time,      บ
 บ  Prophet is not merely being accused of stealing a crack, Prophet is       บ
 บ  accused of attempting to steal an entire game from the Epic cracker,      บ
 บ  Sharp.  The following log file was made in channel #Napalm and should     บ
 บ  shed light on the matter revealing the true character of Prophet and the  บ
 บ  ideals of Napalm.  This time, the evidence is here.                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : The Renegade Chemist                                          บ
 บ    Subject : Prestige & Dynamix - The REAL Story                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      By now many of you may have heard rumors about what caused some of    บ
 บ  the members of Dynamix to join Prestige.  Others of you may not have      บ
 บ  heard them yet, and you might never hear about it.  So I've decided to    บ
 บ  set the record straight before it can get distorted.                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      It's no secret that I haven't been truly active in a long, long       บ
 บ  time.  However, I always tried to keep myself informed of the goings-on   บ
 บ  in the scene, what groups are best, etc., and tried to keep Zeus going    บ
 บ  getting the inside titles that he's able to pull with little effort.  As  บ
 บ  a member of Dynamix, it became clear to me over time that Dynamix was     บ
 บ  going nowhere fast.                                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I planned to start putting forth more effort in the summer, when I    บ
 บ  would only be occupied with work, not school AND work.  Anyway, I         บ
 บ  started by giving Zeus a few phone calls and telling him about some       บ
 บ  upcoming games, Duke Nukem 3D among them.  Zeus bagged Duke Nukem 3D and  บ
 บ  Dynamix was revived after its 2 month "rest" while Crackpot was in        บ
 บ  complete control.                                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      As I became more involved/informed and Zeus dusted off the old        บ
 บ  supply machine, it became increasingly clear that the structure of        บ
 บ  Dynamix was holding it back from becoming something more.  This was       บ
 บ  because the founder of the group, BlueWater, didn't have a phone line     บ
 บ  and even when he did he wasn't much of an organizer, and the guy who'd    บ
 บ  been "running" the group for the past few months (Crackpot) had done      บ
 บ  nothing with it even though he'd had all the opportunity in the world to  บ
 บ  get something accomplished.  I felt that I was in a good position to      บ
 บ  start making moves to improve the group, but like I said, I felt          บ
 บ  constrained by the leadership structure.  Changes were needed, but I      บ
 บ  didn't know exactly how to approach this delicate issue.                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      To make matters worse, neither I nor Zeus really cared for Crackpot.  บ
 บ  At first we tried to work with him, but he seemed to think he knew        บ
 บ  everything better, even to the point where he tried to get himself set    บ
 บ  up with old suppliers who never amounted to much - suppliers like Jack    บ
 บ  from the UK who I've had numerous dealings with in the past, a guy I      บ
 บ  know to be a liar and a thief.  Also, in the 2 months while Zeus and I    บ
 บ  were more or less inactive and in Dynamix, Crackpot had brought in a guy  บ
 บ  from Canada named Hemp Hoodlum to assist him in running the group.        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      So, here was the scenario - Crackpot, Hemp Hoodlum, Zeus, and myself  บ
 บ  were the handful of guys in "charge" of the direction of the group.       บ
 บ  Crackpot/Hemp seemed dedicated to preserving the status quo and maybe     บ
 บ  going out and picking up a few out-of-date suppliers and untested         บ
 บ  crackers.  Zeus wanted to use his methods of supply to get originals and  บ
 บ  start getting the group moving forward again.  I wanted radical changes   บ
 บ  which would allow us to pick up new members who were currently            บ
 บ  producing, and do so in large numbers.  But to do so would contradict     บ
 บ  what Crackpot/Hemp wanted to do with the group, so I was in a quandary.   บ
 บ  But that all changed.                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Speed Master approached me on the Internet and asked me if Dynamix    บ
 บ  would be intersted in a merger with Prestige.  I immediately pondered     บ
 บ  the possibilities - Prestige had a proven UK supply section, a motivated  บ
 บ  US supplier/organizer in Shadow Master, good boards, and also very        บ
 บ  importantly, funding to pay for costs incurred while getting originals.   บ
 บ  They also had several capable crackers which was something that Dynamix   บ
 บ  desperately needed, although we were in the process of picking up some    บ
 บ  guys like Djpaul and had just acquired Holy Beast, 2 solid crackers who   บ
 บ  would add to the mix.  With Dynamix's relatively fluid Internet section,  บ
 บ  along with Zeus, myself, and even Specie picking up the odd title, plus   บ
 บ  any other resources we might have at our disposal, Prestige/Dynamix (as   บ
 บ  it would be called) could truly be a dominating group.  As it turned      บ
 บ  out, that never happened.                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      So after Speed Master suggested the merger, I thought about it and    บ
 บ  called Zeus to see what he thought.  Zeus had a positive opinion, and     บ
 บ  since one of us never does anything without the other, this was an        บ
 บ  important factor.  So, I called Crackpot up and asked him what he         บ
 บ  thought.  I was surprised to find out that this was something that        บ
 บ  Crackpot had been asked about back in March, but he didn't do it then     บ
 บ  for some reason.  Hemp Hoodlum echoed the info that Crackpot had given    บ
 บ  to me.  Crackpot was initially noncommital about the whole thing, but     บ
 บ  Hemp was vehemently in favor of a merger, along with myself and Zeus.     บ
 บ  In any case,3 out of 4 of us were in favor of the merger, with Crackpot   บ
 บ  in a neutral position at this point.  I mentioned earlier that I didn't   บ
 บ  care for Crackpot, but even so, I wanted this merger to happen on the     บ
 บ  best possible terms so I proceeded slowly with it.  Since there were      บ
 บ  only supposed to be 4 of us deciding this kind of thing, and there were   บ
 บ  only 6 active members in Dynamix total anyway, I didn't discuss it with   บ
 บ  anyone else in Dynamix.  Shadow Master was the main person in Prestige    บ
 บ  that I dealt with on the terms of a merger.  We quickly agreed that it    บ
 บ  was not right for the group to still be called Prestige; neither of us    บ
 บ  wanted to see Dynamix absorbed into Prestige, rather the 2 groups were    บ
 บ  to complement each other as a new force.  Shadow Master told me of the    บ
 บ  reluctance of Prestige Europe as well as Zion (sysop of Zion's Hideout)   บ
 บ  to change the name, so we agreed that I would contact the concerned       บ
 บ  parties about this issue.  There was only one other point of contention   บ
 บ  - the new World HQ.  Obviously, Crackpot desired (and expected) that      บ
 บ  Park Central would be the WHQ.  I didn't really care which board was      บ
 บ  WHQ, but if the truth be known, I didn't care for Park Central any more   บ
 บ  than I cared for its cosysop.                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      So, when I was informed by Shadow Master that the deal would fall     บ
 บ  through if Zion's wasn't the WHQ, I knew that I'd have a hard time        บ
 บ  breaking it to Crackpot, but I also knew that in political terms, if      บ
 บ  Crackpot was left out in the cold it wouldn't be a problem.  Hemp, Zeus   บ
 บ  and I seemed unified in that we wanted the merger; it would provide       บ
 บ  fresh blood and fresh ideas that would allow the new group to really      บ
 บ  kick ass.  In any event we didn't want to keep Dynamix going the way      บ
 บ  that it was, and as I mentioned earlier I was a definite proponent of     บ
 บ  quick, sweeping changes in the group.                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      By this time, several days had gone by since the idea of a merger     บ
 บ  had first been broached, and even Crackpot was warming up to it.  He      บ
 บ  still had some reservations about it, the first among them being his      บ
 บ  power in the group (he constantly stated how we needed to enter the       บ
 บ  merger with the "upper hand" - thinking that I did not agree with him)    บ
 บ  and of course the status of his board.  But when I approached him with    บ
 บ  the 2 major points, those being that (a) Zion's would have to be the WHQ  บ
 บ  and (b) the group name would have to be a coop name, ie                   บ
 บ  Prestige/Dynamix, he immediately lost all interest in the merger.  The    บ
 บ  problem was that he didn't tell me that he had lost all interest, so I    บ
 บ  continued to try to convince him that it was the best idea so that we     บ
 บ  could have his blessing rather than his grudging agreement that we were   บ
 บ  doing the right thing.  In the meantime, he went behind my back and       บ
 บ  started to dismantle the merger before we even got it finalized.  He did  บ
 บ  this by talking to other members such as Specie who really had no         บ
 บ  business deciding the direction the group would head in, and he           บ
 บ  convinced them that the merger was only my idea, and that the prime       บ
 บ  reason driving me to push the group into the merger was my desire to be   บ
 บ  able to brag that I was in the best group.  Whether I'm only interested   บ
 บ  in bragging rights isn't the issue at this point; the problem was that    บ
 บ  he was telling me one thing and telling others another altogether.  He    บ
 บ  contined with his story by telling Hemp Hoodlum to cancel the merger.  I  บ
 บ  mean the guy didn't even have the balls to do it himself.  Anyway...      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      So for several days I spoke to Crackpot for at least an hour a day    บ
 บ  extolling to him the virtues of Prestige/Dynamix.  All of the objections  บ
 บ  he posed were totally unfounded, but I can't name all of them here        บ
 บ  because of issues of group secrecy.  One that I CAN discuss, however, is  บ
 บ  his stupid excuse that the group would be lame because the name was       บ
 บ  lame.  Another was that "Dynamix is just starting to be a good group,     บ
 บ  let's not ruin it by joining into a larger one" when in reality it was    บ
 บ  only Zeus who was keeping the group afloat by putting out Duke Nukem 3D.  บ
 บ  When Crackpot started throwing out excuses like that it was pretty clear  บ
 บ  to me that the only real interest he had in the group was to keep it      บ
 บ  right where it was, namely a support group for Park Central.  It was at   บ
 บ  that point that I decided that whether or not the merger occurred, I      บ
 บ  wouldn't be in plain old Dynamix much longer.                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      While I left Crackpot to mull over the information that I'd given     บ
 บ  him, I still had one more detail to sew up - apparently some of the UK    บ
 บ  suppliers were opposed to changing the Prestige name, one that they'd     บ
 บ  built up over a period of 2 1/2 years going back to the Amiga scene.      บ
 บ  Having been a member of a group for an extended period of time (Razor     บ
 บ  1911, 3 1/2 years) I certainly understood their position, and at this     บ
 บ  point I was starting to feel that the merge wasn't going to work out,     บ
 บ  but when I spoke to Deathknight (Euro Prestige leader) I still insisted   บ
 บ  that we have the name Prestige/Dynamix so that Dynamix wouldn't just be   บ
 บ  absorbed into the Prestige infrastructure.  I found out from Deathknight  บ
 บ  that he, and even Zion, were totally unopposed to using a coop name,      บ
 บ  even a new name, and that the only stumbling block were the UK guys.  He  บ
 บ  said that he'd try to convice them and would be back in touch.  Since I   บ
 บ  felt that I still had some convincing to do on my end, I figured I'd let  บ
 บ  it sit over the weekend and by Sunday or Monday we should have something  บ
 บ  set in stone.                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Well, the next day I got on the net and started chatting with Shadow  บ
 บ  Master.  I told him that I had spoken to Deathknight and was awaiting     บ
 บ  his return so that I could finish up with the merger deal with him, when  บ
 บ  SMaster told me that Hemp Hoodlum had told him that the deal was off.     บ
 บ  Of course I was pretty pissed off, and it just so happened that Hemp was  บ
 บ  on IRC so I jumped into a private chat with him and asked what the hell   บ
 บ  was going on.  He told me that Crackpot had told him that I was telling   บ
 บ  people all these different stories in order to seize power in the group   บ
 บ  and force the merger, and that because of that Crackpot had told him to   บ
 บ  put the merger on hold indefinitely.  Upon hearing this I immediately     บ
 บ  told Hemp Hoodlum that I was quitting the group and exited chat.          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Why did I quit so suddenly?  Not because the merger had been placed   บ
 บ  on hold, that was certainly reparable.  The problem I had was that Hemp   บ
 บ  and Crackpot had acted alone without even consulting me (and at this      บ
 บ  point I suspected that they hadn't told Zeus, either).  Since it had      บ
 บ  been agreed that the 4 of us would make the decisions concerning the      บ
 บ  direction of the group, I felt that Crackpot was trying to shut me out    บ
 บ  of the situation so that he could keep Dynamix right where he wanted it   บ
 บ  most - on Park Central, and in his thrall.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I phoned Zeus right away and told him that Hemp/Crackpot had called   บ
 บ  off the deal.  Before I even told him that I had already quit the group,  บ
 บ  Zeus suggested that we both quit Dynamix and join Prestige.  So I knew    บ
 บ  that Zeus wasn't making his decision just based on what I wanted him to   บ
 บ  do.  After Zeus and I had decided that we would indeed leave Dynamix for  บ
 บ  Prestige, I called up a few local friends that I had gotten into Dynamix  บ
 บ  (Bababooey, The Comet) and they agreed to come with us to Prestige also   บ
 บ  - they realized that without Zeus, Dynamix was a sinking ship.  Of        บ
 บ  course Marauder and Randall Flagg came along as well - they didn't even   บ
 บ  have to be asked.  Marauder, RF, Zeus and myself have been friends since  บ
 บ  the beginning of time, and we stay together no matter what.               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      So after I'd determined who would leave in the initial wave (I still  บ
 บ  had to talk to another good friend, Excessive Knight, who has been out    บ
 บ  of the country for some time and unavailable via phone), I called         บ
 บ  Crackpot and told him that we were leaving.  Crackpot was extremely       บ
 บ  bitter and stated his belief that I was worthless and that I was only     บ
 บ  doing it so that I would be in the best group, and that I didn't care     บ
 บ  about anyone else, etc etc etc.  I tried to show him the light, that I    บ
 บ  wanted to be in a group that could kick ass, that Zeus wanted the same,   บ
 บ  and that besides, out of all the people in Dynamix most of us weren't     บ
 บ  friends anyway, but finally I just dropped it and told him that he could  บ
 บ  believe whatever he wanted to, this would be the way it was and that was  บ
 บ  it.                                                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      You can imagine my surprise when Shadow Master told me that as soon   บ
 บ  as I quit IRC, Hemp Hoodlum presented himself and told SMaster that he    บ
 บ  and the remaining Dynamix members would join Prestige if it meant         บ
 บ  keeping me and Zeus out.  SMaster kind of laughed at him.  Later on,      บ
 บ  however, Tazman asked me if I'd mind if Hemp Hoodlum joined the group as  บ
 บ  the two of them were friends.  Even though Hemp had kind of screwed me,   บ
 บ  and I gave Hemp a little shit about it, I figured that he was just        บ
 บ  acting as Crackpot's lackey so I didn't have any real objections to him   บ
 บ  being in the group.  This is where it starts to get a little bit          บ
 บ  confusing.                                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Hemp joined right after our little group of members did, so I wasn't  บ
 บ  really well informed on the whole situation with him.  Boy, was I ever    บ
 บ  shocked to see the next Prestige release that had a whole LOT of members  บ
 บ  in it.  Apparently Hemp Hoodlum misrepresented the whole thing to these   บ
 บ  people and told them that it was in fact a MERGER; and that was just the  บ
 บ  people that he spoke to before putting them in the nfo file.  You can     บ
 บ  imagine I had a little mess to clean up when someone like The Outlaws     บ
 บ  tells me in IRC that Hemp Hoodlum didn't even tell him about the merger   บ
 บ  initially, and that he was surprised to see his name in the nfo file!     บ
 บ  The Outlaws later spoke to Hemp, and like I said was told that there had  บ
 บ  been a merger and that he would retain his German HQ position and even    บ
 บ  become a member.  This was the same story I heard from other people       บ
 บ  ranging from the trader Razor Sharp to the cracker Holy Beast, all these  บ
 บ  people were misinformed by Hemp Hoodlum.  Incidentally, Hemp Hoodlum      บ
 บ  later quit the group, I imagine out of frustration.  The free ride was    บ
 บ  over.                                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      And that's the point of this whole essay.  Dynamix was a joke, but    บ
 บ  when it did "work" it was a free ride for people like Crackpot and Hemp   บ
 บ  Hoodlum.  It really is unfortunate because some people really did         บ
 บ  contribute honestly to the group's success; people like Specie,           บ
 บ  Excessive Knight, and a handful of others.  The problem was that when     บ
 บ  push came to shove, the leadership in place was more interested in        บ
 บ  preserving the status quo and their power than they were in expanding     บ
 บ  the good fortunes of the group.  The free ride is indeed over.            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Road Rebel                                                    บ
 บ    Subject : An Uncontroled IRC Op                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      IRC ops were first created as a form of controlling what happens on   บ
 บ  the IRC network so that things don't get out of hand, and when they do,   บ
 บ  there would be a way of controlling it.  The definition of an IRC op is   บ
 บ  a person that is an administrator of a certain IRC server, and has the    บ
 บ  power to "kill" people or "k-line" people from the network.  A "kill" is  บ
 บ  like a normal channel kick, but it will completely disconnect you from    บ
 บ  the server you're on, meaning that you'll have to reconnect to it, a big  บ
 บ  hassle.  A "k-line" is a banning of a user from a particular server.      บ
 บ  Just as one can get banned from a channel, a person can get banned from   บ
 บ  use of an IRC server.  IRC ops were meant to be regulatory agents of      บ
 บ  IRC, but apparently many IRC ops have been greatly abusing their power,   บ
 บ  breaking into others' channels by killing all the ops, and taking things  บ
 บ  into their own hands, when they "feel" like it.                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Prae, an IRC op, entered channel #RCN when he had a problem with      บ
 บ  Eraser.  Eraser was not even an op in channel #RCN.  #RCN was packed      บ
 บ  with regular channel ops, assigned by the RCN staff to regulate the       บ
 บ  goings-on in the channel, and it would in no way be the business of an    บ
 บ  IRC op to join the channel and impose private regulations upon it.  RCN   บ
 บ  is in no way illegal, we are merely excercising our freedom of speech,    บ
 บ  and thus, at the time, we were in no violation of any of the rules        บ
 บ  behind IRC, nor were we ever caught doing so in the past.  Though there   บ
 บ  are no real written rules for IRC, nor is there a written constitution    บ
 บ  for IRC ops to abide by, it takes just a bit of common sense to figure    บ
 บ  out what they are, and not much more than that to figure out when an IRC  บ
 บ  op is going over his understood boundaries.  In this incident, Eraser     บ
 บ  and Prae started arguing, and Prae was asked to leave.  He was asked      บ
 บ  about 5 times.                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      When he finally had to be banned and kicked, he killed all channel    บ
 บ  ops saying that they were bots.  Generally an IRC op will have to         บ
 บ  justify kills and k-lines so that other IRC ops (to which all kills are   บ
 บ  reported) would know if that op is going too far.  It's sort of a checks  บ
 บ  and balances system, but obviously one that can easily be bypassed, and   บ
 บ  since a jury of IRC ops is never present to assess a situation, it is     บ
 บ  nearly impossible to do anything to fight back against these IRC ops      บ
 บ  "gone bad."  I would like to say that I am not a bot.  Channel #RCN is    บ
 บ  not a warez channel.  Prae was not provoked in anyway.  He was just       บ
 บ  asked to leave, and next to a request such as that, Prae can be           บ
 บ  juxtaposed with any other member of the IRC network, with no              บ
 บ  distinction.                                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      After we got the channel back, he deopped us and took it again, once  บ
 บ  more with no provocation.  There are about 35 witnesses to this that      บ
 บ  agree it is abuse of his oper powers to take a channel because he isn't   บ
 บ  welcome there.  Please take the time to at least read about how Prae      บ
 บ  takes advantages of his position, and how he too, could once again, take  บ
 บ  advantage of us all.                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ

 บ  <PForm> RCN is lame.  No, don't spread logs, it'll end up in RCN.         บ

 บ          stupid group RCN.                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ              what Razor 1911 did.  Who has a log?                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Arch-Vile> Dude, I didn't take a log.  Go ask someone who did.           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <SpeedMstr> I never even got to argue with TSR.  As soon as TSR joined    บ
 บ              the channel, everyone attacked him like a pack of wolves.     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Arch-Vile> Fear this, the latest scoop, Tklp started a new group called  บ
 บ              Reflux.                                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Tklp> No I didn't.                                                       บ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : The Rippa                                                     บ
 บ    Subject : A Little Injustice                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      So here's my little story, the Sunday that RCN #21 was released, I    บ
 บ  decided to go to bed early at around 9:00 pm because I just had a long    บ
 บ  day of trading.  Then, at around 10:05 pm, erie.net (my Internet Service  บ
 บ  Provider), calls my house and asks my brother...                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Disgruntled Sysop> Is (my name) there?                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <My Brother> No, he's sleeping.                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Disgruntled Sysop> I KNOW he's up, let me talk to him NOW!               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      My brother comes in and wakes me up.  I answer the phone and this     บ
 บ  disgruntled bitch starts pissing and moaning about "Someone is making     บ
 บ  fake accounts under my name."  She also threatens to sue me and shit.     บ
 บ  So I say "Look lady, I've been sleeping since 9:00 pm and haven't been    บ
 บ  on since 5:00.  Leave me alone!"  So she hangs up on me, I dial them up,  บ
 บ  and I chat with the sysop...                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  *** SYSOP CHAT MODE ACTIVATED ***                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Sysop> Yes?                                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Me> You tell me what the hell is going on.                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Sysop> Someone going by the name John Doe (my name ommited for safety)   บ
 บ          and THEN kept making fake accounts on our system for over 15 to   บ
 บ          20 minutes.                                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Me> Well, ask my family, I've been taking a nap since 9:00 pm.           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Sysop> OK, I think we already established that it might not have been    บ
 บ          you, but it WAS someone using the same name.  So I did what I am  บ
 บ          expected to do here and call the number listed and verify the     บ
 บ          account.  We do that now for all trial accounts anyway before     บ
 บ          any access is given.                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Me> What you did wasn't a nice friendly call to "verify" an account.     บ
 บ       You threatened to sue me even though "I haven't been on since        บ
 บ       5:00."                                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Sysop> I'm sorry you didn't find it friendly enough, but we've had       บ
 บ          little kids continually calling and setting up bogus accounts     บ
 บ          out of the phone book.  I was actually the friendliest you would  บ
 บ          have found here because I just issued a warning and let you know  บ
 บ          that if it WAS you, that you better stop.  Other sysops might     บ
 บ          have handled it differently.  Soooo, if you aren't to blame,      บ
 บ          then I suggest you just forget about it since you're not the      บ
 บ          guilty party.  If you are, then you shouldn't do it again         บ
 บ          because you could get into trouble.                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Me> Well, I've put up with so much shiznit from you guys that I may be   บ
 บ       moving to ncinter.net shortly.                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Sysop> If you feel that you would be better served, then I wouldn't      บ
 บ          stop you from switching your account.  You might find that they   บ
 บ          won't put up with much either.                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  *** Note : They think my friend hacked them.                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Me> Whatever.  By the way, did that C program I sent you guys help in    บ
 บ       finding that bug in your little security system??                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  *** Note : About 3 minutes pass.                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Me> Still there?                                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Sysop> Yes, I am.  I am speaking to the billing person in the office     บ
 บ          who happens to be one of the owners.  He agrees with me that I    บ
 บ          did what I was supposed to do, and we don't care how many         บ
 บ          accounts a person creates because we have to voice verify every   บ
 บ          one before they are given any access.                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Me> Well I just think next time if you're going to send some... what's   บ
 บ       the word... "sysop trainee" to come flame me over the phone, they    บ
 บ       could be a little bit more polite.                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Sysop> I'm not going to waste my time with you.                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  I decided to cancel my account, and here's my cancellation email :        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Subject : Cancellation                                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      After this billing month, I want to quit your crappy little BBS.      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      By the way, Hydro didn't hack your "firewall."  Just thought I would  บ
 บ  let you guys know of another injustice that happened to another hacker    บ
 บ  just minding his own business.                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                               Signed,                      บ
 บ                                                  The Rippa                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

    ฿฿        ฐ       ฿฿฿ฐ                      ฐ฿฿฿
     ฿ ฿  ฿฿  ฿฿฿   ฿    ฿  r c n          ฿฿ ฿฿
   ฿ ฐ  ฿               ฿   ฿ฐ   ฿
 ฐ ฐฐ ฐ ฿ฐ ฐ฿ ฿ ฐ  ฿฿฿฿฿฿฿ ฐ ฐฐฐฐฐฐ ฐฐฐ
        ฿        ฐ฿฿฿฿฿฿   ฿       ฿
