 ฿ฐ      ฿ฐ      ฿฿฿ฐ                                 ฿฿฿
      ฿                   ฿            a r t i c l e s !
                    ฐ฿                 ฐ฿
                     ฿                   ฿

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Hitex                                                         บ
 บ    Subject : Reflux Made a Boooo Boooo                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      For those of you that don't already know the story, I will go over    บ
 บ  it in an attempt to clarify what is going on.  A short while ago, an old  บ
 บ  group, ROR, decided to call it quits after having their releases banned   บ
 บ  from all the big boards.  This was a result of their releases, as a       บ
 บ  general statement, not working, or being releases nobody would use.       บ
 บ  Tklp thought he would be smart and he renamed the group to Reflux,        บ
 บ  taking in several new members.  His decision paid off, the scene          บ
 บ  accepted Reflux and gave it another chance, still understanding that it   บ
 บ  was basically the same thing.  On one of Reflux's first releases, they    บ
 บ  put out "Bermuda Syndrome," a wonderful Windows 95 game.  However,        บ
 บ  Bermuda Syndrome had already been released by FBI in November of last     บ
 บ  year.  The game slipped through their dupe checking department.  Though   บ
 บ  it caught many eyes and raised many eyebrows as a result of Reflux's      บ
 บ  already marred reputation from ROR, people let it go when Manic, a        บ
 บ  Reflux senior, released a text file (cheap trick for keeping it from      บ
 บ  making it too far past the Internet ;-) apologizing for their mistake.    บ
 บ  It was a respectable apology and was taken in a good way.  People         บ
 บ  understood that people make mistakes, and these guys just made a lot of   บ
 บ  them, this soon after the Quake scandal in which they just edited the     บ
 บ  dates on files to make them look like a different release.                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Today, another member of Reflux released the following text file      บ
 บ  attempting to con the scene into believing that the release was in fact   บ
 บ  NOT a dupe and that it should be regarded as a great release by this      บ
 บ  already shaky group.  Note that I'm writing this article because Rebel    บ
 บ  Chicken is falling out of his chair of laughter and is too amused to      บ
 บ  write it himself.                                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  EXPLANATION                                                               บ
 บ  -----------                                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Here is Jda of RLX. I will try to keep it short: this TXT is to inform,   บ
 บ  not about a poetry :P. A few days ago RLX released:                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  - BERMUDA SYNDROME (c) CENTURY/BGM                                        บ
 บ    a) main (50 disks);                                                     บ
 บ    b) intro/outro add-on;                                                  บ
 บ    c) speech/gfx add-on;                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  In a 30 minutes it turned out that a group called US and FBI released     บ
 บ  that game months ago. We were told we did a dupe. Our senior [-Manic-],   บ
 บ  in order to save RLX's good name, released an official apology. That was  บ
 บ  a right thing to do in that time, but now we want to explain *all*        บ
 บ  details and get over this accident...                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  ...because in a fact BERMUDA SYNDROME was not a dupe. Here is how:        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  1. We have released *different* version, version 1.2. Just look at the    บ
 บ     patch included in PATCH.ZIP on the first disk. Apart from this: the    บ
 บ     old version had around 186 megs on CD, ours has around 220 megs. The   บ
 บ     old release is in Russian, ours is in *English*. In our version the    บ
 บ     dialogues are different also, when you look at the old release you     บ
 บ     will see.                                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  2. The reasons for the above changes is that the game is about to be      บ
 บ     released in the West. The game was written by Russians, and Western    บ
 บ     people demanded changes (animations, dialogues, etc.). BERMUDA         บ
 บ     SYNDROME is now being advertised in UK press, for example. So the old  บ
 บ     release was just some kind of test version, and we have released the   บ
 บ     final thing.                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  3. Old release version was over 60 disks. In that times the disk limit    บ
 บ     for a release was 30 or 40 disks, I do not remember, never mind. Now   บ
 บ     it is 50 disks. Still *very* far from 60... SO THE OLD RELEASE SHOULD  บ
 บ     BE TREATED AS NON-EXISTANT! This is just a simple logic: scene has     บ
 บ     its rules and we have to listen to them. If disk limit is exceeded,    บ
 บ     then release is a fuckup and noone should give a fuck about it.        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  In other words: RLX released *correctly* stripped version (not exceeding  บ
 บ  the disk limit), in *proper* language (English speech and English         บ
 บ  dialogues translated by our bro Alchemist), and in *latest* version       บ
 บ  (1.2, which is supposed to be final).                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  The game would be GAME OF THE WEEK in Ionizer's Games Review, if not the  บ
 บ  scene, which jumped on us screaming it is a dupe. This the simply the     บ
 บ  best Windows'95-only game I ever saw, and we just cannot let it go. We    บ
 บ  would not sacrifice a *very* hard work of a few people (ripping,          บ
 บ  cracking, translating) just because of old, lame, 61 disk release of      บ
 บ  Russian version.                                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  I can imagine a few you who now think to themselves: "Geez, fuck RLX,     บ
 บ  they did a dupe, they cannot be trusted because of RoR's fuckups, they    บ
 บ  cannot see the sad truth, they should be banned" etc. To those people     บ
 บ  all I can say is: read my explanation again. Think about it. Do not be    บ
 บ  biased.                                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  And finally: the release was supplied by very close friend of game's      บ
 บ  main programmer. Here is what his friend T0k, president of util group     บ
 บ  SODOM, has to say about it:                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  "                                                                         บ
 บ  Hi.                                                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  So, i wanna tell u someffin about this release from reflux... all u know  บ
 บ  it was released from FBI... Bermuda Syndrome few months ago...  but:      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  1. 1st thing why u must belive me: `coz i know *PERSONALY* ppl from       บ
 บ     company who coded this game, in russia, and i was 1st who get this     บ
 บ     game... i mean i was 1st on scene who take it in hand, so, tell me     บ
 บ     now, why the fuck, i need to release twice??? sure reflux released     บ
 บ     new version of Bermuda! ask yourself, why i didn't i hear about this   บ
 บ     game before??? if it is so fucking cool, as Ionizer write in review    บ
 บ     about it??? i can tell u why... `coz "FBI" release shit...             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    -- non working version... like beta or someffin...                      บ
 บ    -- without English patch... *russian language only*                     บ
 บ    -- lame rip...                                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  that's why noone heard about this briliant game... IMHO best arcade game  บ
 บ  for windows 95 for last few months. And when some ppl tell me the game    บ
 บ  was nuked, `coz siteops or someone see JUST "BERMUDA SYNDROME" and        บ
 บ  thinks that was a dupe... so... look, this release from reflux was realy  บ
 บ  decent, and i'm glad to tell u, that most part of europen siteop, don't   บ
 บ  nuke it, and understand that was good/new one, u'll see it when they run  บ
 บ  it, and n`joy... so... in the future... if u wanna scream/nuke someffin,  บ
 บ  just cheek it out 1st... and don't panic... ok, thats all this time.      บ
 บ  thx.                                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                -- TOk.                                     บ
 บ  "                                                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  CONCLUSION:                                                               บ
 บ  -----------                                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  BERMUDA SYNDROME was *not* a dupe. Anyway, we are releasing this *final*  บ
 บ  explanation just to clear things up, not to start a war or anything.      บ
 บ  When you will be safely enjoying BERMUDA, knowing that it is OK release,  บ
 บ  we will strike again with another game. Because that is what we are for.  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                               JdA/RLX      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Now for the part where I tell you that this is complete bull shit     บ
 บ  and should have actually been in Mad RCN because it's so amusing.  I      บ
 บ  have great respect for Manic because he just got up and made an apology   บ
 บ  to the scene for a mistake.  I'm sure the general concencus among Reflux  บ
 บ  members upon finding out that they duped was a shiver here, a shiver      บ
 บ  there, an "oh crap" here and another there.  Manic suppressed the fear    บ
 บ  and just said the truth, apparently while JdA was coming up with a good   บ
 บ  lie that he thought the scene would believe -- very unprofessional.       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Obviously there are some huge leaps that JdA ignored while writing    บ
 บ  his file.  Generally if a game company wants to release a new version of  บ
 บ  a game, they'll do so and name the version 2.0.  That is, the game will   บ
 บ  be a bit different, like JdA said.  However, this wasn't the case with    บ
 บ  this game.  Perhaps the game was a different version, I could buy the     บ
 บ  verison 1.2 business, after all I have no way of verifying it now, as 8   บ
 บ  months is a bit late to go looking on sites, but if that's the case, and  บ
 บ  if you could fit a patch on one disk, WHY THE HELL DIDN'T YOU JUST        บ
 บ  RELEASE THE PATCH?                                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Also, don't try to say the old release is non-existent, FBI never     บ
 บ  agreed to any disk limit 8 months ago, and neither did ROR/RLX now,       บ
 บ  because you guys were not invited to the meetings regarding it.  So       บ
 บ  don't try to justify yourself by claiming others' faults.  If anybody's   บ
 บ  release should be claimed non-existent, it's yours, because you're the    บ
 บ  one that said you had one of your own guys translate the game, and last   บ
 บ  I checked the warez scene releases software by the companies, not half    บ
 บ  by the companies and half the group's work.  RLX is lucky because ROR     บ
 บ  was granted a second chance, but don't expect old views of ROR to be      บ
 บ  lost, you weren't granted a new life, just a new name and a second        บ
 บ  chance.                                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Finally, if this hasn't convinced you yet, please explain the file    บ
 บ  dates.  The file dates still said October 1995, which sounds a lot like   บ
 บ  the FBI release.  You guys did a better job on the Quake cop out, at      บ
 บ  least there you faked the dates, you didn't even do THAT for this         บ
 บ  release.                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I hate to break it to you but Reflux is already banned from Beyond    บ
 บ  Akira, and I shudder to think about how many more boards that ban could   บ
 บ  be extended to.  Next time take more responsibility for your actions.     บ
 บ  And JdA, Manic has guts, you're just fluff.  Your group doesn't           บ
 บ  necessarily represent you, but you always represent your group, and       บ
 บ  you're making a fool out of Reflux.  I just hope that people will         บ
 บ  disregard your lame excuse for a rebuttal and listen to Manic's one.      บ
 บ  Reflux duped, they made an honest mistake, and did more than most groups  บ
 บ  would after a dupe, they apologized.                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

      ฿                   ฿            a r t i c l e s !

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Midnight Avian                                                บ
 บ    Subject : "Is that box really important to you?"                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      It might sound kind of weird to pick a machine over your friends but  บ
 บ  to some of us, that's reality.  How many of you spend more time on your   บ
 บ  computer than seeing your friends or talk to your friends?  In the old    บ
 บ  days, you'd ask a friend for help when you were feeling upset.  Nowadays  บ
 บ  you just start couriering your head off and you keep your problem to      บ
 บ  yourself.  That's not healthy!  I bet that most of you don't even need    บ
 บ  most of the stuff that you download!  Maybe you'll want the odd game,     บ
 บ  maybe a ten mes release or so but comparing to the useless stuff you've   บ
 บ  couriered, it's nothing.  At this rate, no one will even speak by the     บ
 บ  year 2000!  Think about it!  When you have a problem, talk about it with  บ
 บ  someone.  Don't just type "/msg ???-DCC xdcc send #1"!                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I remember when I had a girlfriend, she would sometimes ask me, "Is   บ
 บ  that box really important to you?"  I would just laugh and avoid the      บ
 บ  question.  After all, what can I say?  Should I say, "Yes, it's more      บ
 บ  important than you!"  Or should I say, "Nah, I don't even use it that     บ
 บ  much!"?                                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      There's one thing you have to remember, you bought the computer and   บ
 บ  the computer is owned by YOU.  Computers can be part of your life but     บ
 บ  shouldn't take over your life.  If you're bored then fool around on the   บ
 บ  computer but if you've got something to do, do it!  Don't play IRC and    บ
 บ  not do what you have to do.  Life's short, have fun!  Sex, party,         บ
 บ  movies, more sex is far more interesting than looking at the scene that   บ
 บ  changes images every second.                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Being a courier myself, sometimes I ask.  "Why do I courier?"  The    บ
 บ  answer is often unknown.  People courier because of different reasons.    บ
 บ  Some people will be happy if they have fast warez to upload.  Some        บ
 บ  people just do it because they have nothing better to do.  Some people    บ
 บ  might think that couriers are jerks that have no life and just sit in     บ
 บ  front of the computer and wait for uploads and downloads to be done.  I   บ
 บ  have three words for these people, "Shame on you!"  Without these         บ
 บ  people, the files would not move around nearly as quickly as they do      บ
 บ  now, and also, if there were no couriers in the world, the warez scene    บ
 บ  would not grow as quickly as it has.                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      My friend always tells me that I have no life when couriering and I   บ
 บ  say, "What is meant by no life, if it's not going out, then I do have a   บ
 บ  life because I go out with my friends a hell of a lot more than you!"     บ
 บ  You don't have to be in front of the computer when you courier, you can   บ
 บ  be watching TV, going out with friends, having sex.  Even studying if     บ
 บ  you're bored enough!  So next time you want to insult a courier, not      บ
 บ  like anyone would have the guts to because there are millions of          บ
 บ  couriers out there, just think twice about it.                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Rebel Chicken                                                 บ
 บ    Subject : Group Reviews : Games                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Hello, and welcome to Reality Check Network's all new group review!   บ
 บ  Here I will be reviewing the 5 best games release groups in the scene.    บ
 บ  Well, actually, *I* won't be the one reviewing them, *THEY* will be!      บ
 บ  It's all up to the groups, this is where quantity DOES count, but you     บ
 บ  will soon enough find that quality by far outweighs quantity.  Let's      บ
 บ  review the criteria I'll be using for judging releases.  The following    บ
 บ  is the scoring basis I'll be using :                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Points :                                                                  บ
 บ  --------                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [-3] The game didn't work and a crack/fix was not released within 72      บ
 บ       hours.  The group may regain the 3 lost points by releasing a crack  บ
 บ       or fix, even beyond the 3 day period.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 1] The game was a dupe or freeware,                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 2] Unsatisfactory,                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 3] Average,                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 4] Above Average, and                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 5] Excellent!                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A group may lose points the following week and have their releases    บ
 บ  labeled as broken (thus receiving the proper amout of points).  If the    บ
 บ  group has released a fix between the two issues, we'll give them credit   บ
 บ  accordingly.  If a group releases a fix within a 3 day period, the        บ
 บ  game will be rated as if it worked in the first place, thus getting the   บ
 บ  3 points it lost back and any points it would have earned.  If a group    บ
 บ  releases a fix after the 3 day period has expired, it will receive its 3  บ
 บ  points back, but get no more.  Betas may receive no more than 3 points.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Rebel Chicken                                                 บ
 บ    Subject : Group Reviews : Games                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Hello, and welcome to Reality Check Network's all new group review!   บ
 บ  Here I will be reviewing the 5 best games release groups in the scene.    บ
 บ  Well, actually, *I* won't be the one reviewing them, *THEY* will be!      บ
 บ  It's all up to the groups, this is where quantity DOES count, but you     บ
 บ  will soon enough find that quality by far outweighs quantity.  Let's      บ
 บ  review the criteria I'll be using for judging releases.  The following    บ
 บ  is the scoring basis I'll be using :                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Points :                                                                  บ
 บ  --------                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [-3] The game didn't work and a crack/fix was not released within 72      บ
 บ       hours.  The group may regain the 3 lost points by releasing a crack  บ
 บ       or fix, even beyond the 3 day period.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 1] The game was a dupe or freeware,                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 2] Unsatisfactory,                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 3] Average,                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 4] Above Average, and                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 5] Excellent!                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A group may lose points the following week and have their releases    บ
 บ  labeled as broken (thus receiving the proper amout of points).  If the    บ
 บ  group has released a fix between the two issues, we'll give them credit   บ
 บ  accordingly.  If a group releases a fix within a 3 day period, the        บ
 บ  game will be rated as if it worked in the first place, thus getting the   บ
 บ  3 points it lost back and any points it would have earned.  If a group    บ
 บ  releases a fix after the 3 day period has expired, it will receive its 3  บ
 บ  points back, but get no more.  Betas may receive no more than 3 points.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  ฺฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฟ  บ
 บ  ณ            Dates of Games Reviewed : 06/20/96 -> 06/26/96            ณ  บ
 บ  ภฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤู  บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Rebel Chicken                                                 บ
 บ    Subject : Group Reviews : Games                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Hello, and welcome to Reality Check Network's all new group review!   บ
 บ  Here I will be reviewing the 5 best games release groups in the scene.    บ
 บ  Well, actually, *I* won't be the one reviewing them, *THEY* will be!      บ
 บ  It's all up to the groups, this is where quantity DOES count, but you     บ
 บ  will soon enough find that quality by far outweighs quantity.  Let's      บ
 บ  review the criteria I'll be using for judging releases.  The following    บ
 บ  is the scoring basis I'll be using :                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Points :                                                                  บ
 บ  --------                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [-3] The game didn't work and a crack/fix was not released within 72      บ
 บ       hours.  The group may regain the 3 lost points by releasing a crack  บ
 บ       or fix, even beyond the 3 day period.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 1] The game was a dupe or freeware,                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 2] Unsatisfactory,                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 3] Average,                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 4] Above Average, and                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 5] Excellent!                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A group may lose points the following week and have their releases    บ
 บ  labeled as broken (thus receiving the proper amout of points).  If the    บ
 บ  group has released a fix between the two issues, we'll give them credit   บ
 บ  accordingly.  If a group releases a fix within a 3 day period, the        บ
 บ  game will be rated as if it worked in the first place, thus getting the   บ
 บ  3 points it lost back and any points it would have earned.  If a group    บ
 บ  releases a fix after the 3 day period has expired, it will receive its 3  บ
 บ  points back, but get no more.  Betas may receive no more than 3 points.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  ฺฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฟ  บ
 บ  ณ            Dates of Games Reviewed : 07/04/96 -> 07/10/96            ณ  บ
 บ  ภฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤู  บ

 บ GAME REVIEWS, RATINGS, UN-BIASED OPINIONS, HELP/TIPS FOR INSTALLING GAMES! บ
 บ [][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][][] บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Rating scale :                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ           (0-19)/100 = In a nutshell, it sucked!                           บ
 บ          (20-39)/100 = Still crap but slightly better.                     บ
 บ          (40-49)/100 = Possibly worth downloading.                         บ
 บ          (50-69)/100 = Pretty decent game. Might want to check it out.     บ
 บ          (70-79)/100 = Worth the download if you like that type.           บ
 บ          (80-89)/100 = Very good, 9 outta 10 its worth the download.       บ
 บ          (90-99)/100 = Excellent game, a MUST download.                    บ
 บ              100/100 = HOLY SHIT I'VE NEVER SEEN A BETTER GAME!            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      RATINGS are based on the game idea, graphics, sound, playability,     บ
 บ  ingenuity, versatility, and a lot of other words ending in 'ity.'  These  บ
 บ  games are based on what happens on MY COMPUTER ONLY, unless stated        บ
 บ  otherwise.  I always first follow NFO directions, and if those don't      บ
 บ  work or are not available, I then try other ways.  So just b/c it         บ
 บ  doesn't work for me, doesn't mean it won't work for you.                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                       -<*><*> THE GAME REVIEW <*><*>-                      บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป                              บ
 บ  บ    18 CLASSIC CASINO GAMES FOR WINDOWS   บ                              บ
 บ  บ                       Sat. July. 6, 1996 บ                              บ
 บ  บ                                    xx/05 บ                              บ
 บ  ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Like it says, this is 18 casino like games for windows.  The          บ
 บ  graphics start off shitty, but you can change them so that they look      บ
 บ  like they came from this century.  Some of the games include the          บ
 บ  following: 7 Card Stud, Bandit, Blackjack, Craps, Dayraces, Draw 5        บ
 บ  Poker, Holdem, Keno, Lotto, One Arm Bandit, Pot of Gold, Roulette, and    บ
 บ  Video Poker.  It certainly is not that nice collection of card games      บ
 บ  that you are looking for.  Dull and boring.  Here is an alternative       บ
 บ  review courtesy of Tornado, I thought it was slightly humorous : "Well    บ
 บ  the games are playable.  The games are 16 colors all of them.  They       บ
 บ  aren't registered.  You have a 30 day trial period which is fine because  บ
 บ  you can't even play this crap that long.  Basically it's for idiots or    บ
 บ  just for people that like any game."                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                               RATING : 22/100                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ   ฿฿฿฿฿    ฿฿฿฿฿ ฿  ฿฿฿                                    บ
 บ  ฿฿     r  e  f  l  u  x  !      ฐฐ                                  บ
 บ   ฿    ฤฤฤฤฤฤ ฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤ-- - -ฤ -ฤฤฤ-ฤ                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Here's the working version of this detective game.  Precision's was   บ
 บ  not cracked or cracked properly, and so Reflux took a crack at it <der    บ
 บ  get it?> and was able to make it work fine w/o the need for               บ
 บ  subst/fakecd.  This is an adventure game involving many interactions      บ
 บ  with characters, and of course, as all good detectives do, looking and    บ
 บ  searching for clues.  The graphics are ok, and you pretty much NEED the   บ
 บ  sound addon in order to play, or else you'll be walking around clueless.  บ
 บ  You really need the full cd for this one, in order to figure out the      บ
 บ  plot, because it uses movies or something that tell the plot (such as a   บ
 บ  guy getting killed) and you need to know what happened.  It's hard to     บ
 บ  play with out them, because you're talking to a guy one minute, and the   บ
 บ  next you see he's dead on the floor, and you missed it all.  One          บ
 บ  annoying thing was when the game tried to load the movies, it would get   บ
 บ  an error, you have to hit ok, and then escape too, and this gets to be    บ
 บ  very annoying.  It might be a good game on CD, but it's not worth it to   บ
 บ  get this rip, because you're missing out on half the game.  Unless you    บ
 บ  plan on buying this one and want to see what it's like, don't waste your  บ
 บ  time.                                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                               RATING : 45/100                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ

 บ  Lemmings Paintball *FiNAL*  [o1/17]                                       บ
 บ  -----------------------------------                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Lemmings Paintball for Win95.  Let's see here.  This game was         บ
 บ  supposedly released earlier by Hybrid, but apparently that version was a  บ
 บ  beta, or a release meant for computer magazines and far from complete.    บ
 บ  The game idea is simple if you can put 2 and 2 together, Lemmings +       บ
 บ  Paintball.  The game is cool, but relatively easy.  It has a multiplayer  บ
 บ  for playing over the net, but is otherwise very easy or very hard         บ
 บ  depending on the settings.  The intro is hilarious, and I'm glad Motiv8   บ
 บ  left it in.  Overall, a good small game with a good rip.                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                   RATING : 80/100 (If you like Lemmings)                   บ
 บ          RATING : 74/100 (If you have another person to play with)         บ
 บ             RATING : 60/100 (If you don't like Lemmings at all)            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ

 บ  <nice .diz>                                                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Tracer for Win95 7th Level                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Install Note: This game was previously screwed, but a fix was         บ
 บ  released (finally..) after about 8 days.  Thanks to PSG for fixing the    บ
 บ  screwup! Just install according to the .nfo in the fixfile.  If ya get    บ
 บ  something to the effect of: "wing32.dll not found" you need to install    บ
 บ  WinG32 included with the fix.  DUH! :)                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Hmmm.  I like it.  Dunno why, but I like it.  This isn't an action    บ
 บ  shooter, but gameplay is fast - due to the virus on your ass wanting to   บ
 บ  eat you up!  It's more strategy than anything.  Ya gotta move from block  บ
 บ  to block laying down tiles to walk on top of as you go.  Simple enough.   บ
 บ  HA! You get a limited amount of tiles AND your previous tiles get eaten   บ
 บ  as you go.  There's some special kinds of tiles that do different         บ
 บ  things, and you can grab power up items on your way to the end of the     บ
 บ  level.  The music rocks with a techno rhythm, and there's clear           บ
 บ  understandable speech at the beginning of each level.  The graphics are   บ
 บ  excellent but don't stop to admire them! There's even pan/zoom options    บ
 บ  to move the view around the game area.                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Points: 82 - All in all, not a bad game.  It's definately different.    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ

 บ       CLOSE COMBAT AMAZING FIX [1/1]                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Ok, now this fix all by itself doesn't work.  I was highly pissed off     บ
 บ  about it too, until Ionizer, Mr.  Ereet himself /msg'd me this in IRC:    บ
 บ  *** Topic for #napalm: Close Combat Fix - ATTRIB -R *.* /S on the         บ
 บ  Install Directory. FINALLY, after all this fiddlefucken around, the game  บ
 บ  works.                                                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      So, to install: Do everything according to the original .nfo (copy    บ
 บ  this fixed .exe instead of the original cracked one), then in the dir     บ
 บ  you ran setup from type "attrib -R *.* /S", try to run the game, when it  บ
 บ  craps out load up regedit and do that, then PLAY!                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      As for the game itself, it pretty much kicks ass.  This isn't your    บ
 บ  run of the mill overhead military battle sim.  In most sims, you put      บ
 บ  troops here, hit a button, and poof they either win or lose.  In this     บ
 บ  one, you can control your troops even after starting the battle (like     บ
 บ  you should be able to), and even tell specific people to do specific      บ
 บ  things (move here, aim there, etc..) You can be either side too.          บ
 บ  Germany pretty much defends and the good ole USA tries to take            บ
 บ  buildings, landmarks, whatever (umm what? so they can give em back        บ
 บ  later??) Your troops can get medals, promotions, etc for getting shot,    บ
 บ  or good work.  I was kinda disappointed that I couldn't call in           บ
 บ  airstrikes, but we got old fashioned mortar maggots to do the job right.  บ
 บ  The sounds were excellent, you hear alot of shit all at once, ppl         บ
 บ  getting shot, radio chatter, mortar fire, tanks, and even a little        บ
 บ  german mixed in..  The help file wasn't included, but there is on-screen  บ
 บ  help during gameplay and alot of the stuff is self explanitory.  Don't    บ
 บ  hit the news reel button after a mission either, it'll crap out looking   บ
 บ  for the video files.  I only played through the first mission (I've       บ
 บ  still got 3 releases to review in about 9 hours, WHILE leechin my ass     บ
 บ  off..ughh), but this is definitely a keeper!                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ            Points : 83 - Get this and play this.  It's worth it!           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ   Bruce Jenner's DECATHLON (c) I-Magic [1/9]                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Remember that old 2600 game Decathalon? heh Not quite that bad.  But in   บ
 บ  some ways, I think the Atari ver beat this one hands down.  Ok, this has  บ
 บ  nice grafix and all, and you can design your chr's attributes, but the    บ
 บ  actual gameplay was pretty crappy.  There just aren't enough controls.    บ
 บ  I was expecting a "fry out 2 joysticks in 8 hours" type of game, but all  บ
 บ  you do is click the mouse when your dude is sposed to do something (like  บ
 บ  jump, or throw..) Not a whole lot to say about this, pretty boring.       บ
 บ  Note: something screwy went on with the sounds, cuz during play, it       บ
 บ  would play sounds from a directX game called Subspace I play over the     บ
 บ  net..  Dunno??                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ        Points : 51 - The only semi-redeeming quality was the grafix.       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ

 บ  Lemmings for Win95          [o1/o1]                                       บ
 บ  -----------------------------------                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Seeing releases like this makes me wonder why in hell I leech 50 disk     บ
 บ  games. One disk for this one.  Period.  Before you come at me with the    บ
 บ  "awww come on, it's LEMMINGS" line, take a look at this game.  There's    บ
 บ  new levels and all the old ones too, good sound, good graphics (Lemmings  บ
 บ  STYLE!), and can be played doing anything in windows (I was leechin in    บ
 บ  QmodemPro while playing this, not one error).  Options include sound      บ
 บ  on/off, level select, high/low rez, zoom, and a couple others.            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      *><* Uninstall: It's a bitch.  If you don't care about having         บ
 บ  "Lemmings.." in the add/remove box for the rest of your life, don't       บ
 บ  worry about it.  I do care so..  You have to copy all files from          บ
 บ  \progra~1\winlemm to \lemmings, then move \lemmings\gfx\logo.bmp to       บ
 บ  \lemmings\pblogo.bmp and then finally type autorun in the \lemmings dir.  บ
 บ  Yucky!                                                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ     Points : 76-5 (uninstall) = 71 Only ONE disk! Good release from the    บ
 บ                          guys of m8.  Keep it up!                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ

 บ      This is one of the best games I've seen for 95 so far.  The only      บ
 บ  thing I don't like is it being 50 disks, but ya get what ya leech I       บ
 บ  guess (hrmm sometimes).  The grafix on this kicks a helluvalotta ass.     บ
 บ  Smooth animation..  I take that back, it's somehow better than smooth.    บ
 บ  It kinda reminds me of Pitfall for 95 but extremely realistic.  The       บ
 บ  soundtrack from what I heard of it, has a damn hard beat to it.  Kicked   บ
 บ  my AWE and woofers into overdrive.  The plot starts out with you saving   บ
 บ  this half naked chic (w00h00) and finding out that you have to get out    บ
 บ  of the jungle alive while saving her father, who just happens to be the   บ
 บ  king.  hmm Maybe I'll play this game to the end to see if ya get to bang  บ
 บ  her or not..  Just way too much good stuff to say about this game tho.    บ
 บ  In case you can't figure it out, try the tab, enter, and space keys.      บ
 บ  The mouse works as a pointer, but the right button takes ya back to the   บ
 บ  main menu.  No real options to speak of, I do wish that it would go full  บ
 บ  screen at 800x600, but I ain't bitchin much, cuz this game ROCKS!         บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Rebel Chicken                                                 บ
 บ    Subject : Group Reviews : Utils                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Hello, and welcome to Reality Check Network's all new group review!   บ
 บ  Here I will be reviewing the 5 best utils release groups in the scene.    บ
 บ  Well, actually, *I* won't be the one reviewing them, *THEY* will be!      บ
 บ  It's all up to the groups, this is where quantity DOES count, but you     บ
 บ  will soon enough find that quality by far outweighs quantity.  Let's      บ
 บ  review the criteria I'll be using for judging releases.  The following    บ
 บ  is the scoring basis I'll be using :                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Points :                                                                  บ
 บ  --------                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [-3] The util didn't work and a crack/fix was not released within 72      บ
 บ       hours.  The group may regain the 3 lost points by releasing a crack  บ
 บ       or fix, even beyond the 3 day period.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 1] The util was a dupe or freeware,                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 2] Unsatisfactory,                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 3] Average,                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 4] Above Average, and                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 5] Excellent!                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A group may lose points the following week and have their releases    บ
 บ  labeled as broken (thus receiving the proper amout of points).  If the    บ
 บ  group has released a fix between the two issues, we'll give them credit   บ
 บ  accordingly.  If a group releases a fix within a 3 day period, the        บ
 บ  util will be rated as if it worked in the first place, thus getting the   บ
 บ  3 points it lost back and any points it would have earned.  If a group    บ
 บ  releases a fix after the 3 day period has expired, it will receive its 3  บ
 บ  points back, but get no more.  Betas may receive no more than 3 points.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  ฺฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฟ  บ
 บ  ณ            Dates of Utils Reviewed : 06/13/96 -> 06/19/96            ณ  บ
 บ  ภฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤู  บ

 บ    Author  : Rebel Chicken                                                 บ
 บ    Subject : Group Reviews : Utils                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Hello, and welcome to Reality Check Network's all new group review!   บ
 บ  Here I will be reviewing the 5 best utils release groups in the scene.    บ
 บ  Well, actually, *I* won't be the one reviewing them, *THEY* will be!      บ
 บ  It's all up to the groups, this is where quantity DOES count, but you     บ
 บ  will soon enough find that quality by far outweighs quantity.  Let's      บ
 บ  review the criteria I'll be using for judging releases.  The following    บ
 บ  is the scoring basis I'll be using :                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Points :                                                                  บ
 บ  --------                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [-3] The util didn't work and a crack/fix was not released within 72      บ
 บ       hours.  The group may regain the 3 lost points by releasing a crack  บ
 บ       or fix, even beyond the 3 day period.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 1] The util was a dupe or freeware,                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 2] Unsatisfactory,                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 3] Average,                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 4] Above Average, and                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 5] Excellent!                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A group may lose points the following week and have their releases    บ
 บ  labeled as broken (thus receiving the proper amout of points).  If the    บ
 บ  group has released a fix between the two issues, we'll give them credit   บ
 บ  accordingly.  If a group releases a fix within a 3 day period, the        บ
 บ  util will be rated as if it worked in the first place, thus getting the   บ
 บ  3 points it lost back and any points it would have earned.  If a group    บ
 บ  releases a fix after the 3 day period has expired, it will receive its 3  บ
 บ  points back, but get no more.  Betas may receive no more than 3 points.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  ฺฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฟ  บ
 บ  ณ            Dates of Utils Reviewed : 06/20/96 -> 06/26/96            ณ  บ

 บ    Subject : Group Reviews : Utils                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Hello, and welcome to Reality Check Network's all new group review!   บ
 บ  Here I will be reviewing the 5 best utils release groups in the scene.    บ
 บ  Well, actually, *I* won't be the one reviewing them, *THEY* will be!      บ
 บ  It's all up to the groups, this is where quantity DOES count, but you     บ
 บ  will soon enough find that quality by far outweighs quantity.  Let's      บ
 บ  review the criteria I'll be using for judging releases.  The following    บ
 บ  is the scoring basis I'll be using :                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Points :                                                                  บ
 บ  --------                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [-3] The util didn't work and a crack/fix was not released within 72      บ
 บ       hours.  The group may regain the 3 lost points by releasing a crack  บ
 บ       or fix, even beyond the 3 day period.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 1] The util was a dupe or freeware,                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 2] Unsatisfactory,                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 3] Average,                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 4] Above Average, and                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 5] Excellent!                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A group may lose points the following week and have their releases    บ
 บ  labeled as broken (thus receiving the proper amout of points).  If the    บ
 บ  group has released a fix between the two issues, we'll give them credit   บ
 บ  accordingly.  If a group releases a fix within a 3 day period, the        บ
 บ  util will be rated as if it worked in the first place, thus getting the   บ
 บ  3 points it lost back and any points it would have earned.  If a group    บ
 บ  releases a fix after the 3 day period has expired, it will receive its 3  บ
 บ  points back, but get no more.  Betas may receive no more than 3 points.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ    Author  : Rebel Chicken                                                 บ
 บ    Subject : Group Reviews : Utils                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Hello, and welcome to Reality Check Network's all new group review!   บ
 บ  Here I will be reviewing the 5 best utils release groups in the scene.    บ
 บ  Well, actually, *I* won't be the one reviewing them, *THEY* will be!      บ
 บ  It's all up to the groups, this is where quantity DOES count, but you     บ
 บ  will soon enough find that quality by far outweighs quantity.  Let's      บ
 บ  review the criteria I'll be using for judging releases.  The following    บ
 บ  is the scoring basis I'll be using :                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Points :                                                                  บ
 บ  --------                                                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [-3] The util didn't work and a crack/fix was not released within 72      บ
 บ       hours.  The group may regain the 3 lost points by releasing a crack  บ
 บ       or fix, even beyond the 3 day period.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 1] The util was a dupe or freeware,                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 2] Unsatisfactory,                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 3] Average,                                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 4] Above Average, and                                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  [ 5] Excellent!                                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      A group may lose points the following week and have their releases    บ
 บ  labeled as broken (thus receiving the proper amout of points).  If the    บ
 บ  group has released a fix between the two issues, we'll give them credit   บ
 บ  accordingly.  If a group releases a fix within a 3 day period, the        บ
 บ  util will be rated as if it worked in the first place, thus getting the   บ
 บ  3 points it lost back and any points it would have earned.  If a group    บ
 บ  releases a fix after the 3 day period has expired, it will receive its 3  บ
 บ  points back, but get no more.  Betas may receive no more than 3 points.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ฬออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออน
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  ฺฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฟ  บ
 บ  ณ            Dates of Utils Reviewed : 07/04/96 -> 07/10/96            ณ  บ
 บ  ภฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤู  บ

 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Okay, this section is good because you get money, LOTS of money.      บ
 บ  Well, this section here is a story, not a "How to", but just follow what  บ
 บ  I do, or vary it, and you'll do fine.  Here goes...                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I needed money, and I needed it FAST.  I wanted to buy some           บ
 บ  hardware.  My computer was getting more and more out dated each DAY.      บ
 บ  New stuff were coming in, and the old were just discarded.  I'd search    บ
 บ  for money under the couch... only pennies.  In my drawers... dimes here.  บ
 บ  Then I thought of using my computer.  By the way, I know what your        บ
 บ  thinking.  I'll answer it right now.  No this is not one of those         บ
 บ  "Fill-out-the-form-as- number-10-and-send-in-$10-and-be-rich" deals, so   บ

 บ  gave them my carding site (a neighbor's home, which they have gone out    บ

 บ  Ripping Phones Off                                                        บ
 บ  ------------------                                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  Note : Blueboxes can't do shit no more, so if you're trying, the only     บ
 บ         thing you'll get is the cool hardware, handcuffs.                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Call 0 and wait for the operator to come on.  Say, "I'm at LaLaLand,  บ
 บ  and I keep putting in my quarters.  They keep coming back.  I need to     บ
 บ  tell my Mom/Dad/Aunt/whoever where to pick me up, and what time.  Can     บ
 บ  you put me through?  This is an Emergency!"  They'll say, "Okay sure,"    บ
 บ  tell them the number, and they'll dial it.  Then you go through.  Nice,   บ
 บ  eh? If the operator says to use collect, say "Okay", and hang-up.  Dial   บ
 บ  0 again and try your luck again.  I've done this at the airport.  Very    บ
 บ  nice.  Many operators give away many free calls.  :)                      บ

 บ  How to Get Money FROM Payphones                                           บ
 บ  -------------------------------                                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      You must select a phone that you can have access to its wires.  Look  บ
 บ  for a plastic shroud running down the wall, or the junction box outside!  บ
 บ  On a normal phoneline, only two wires are used, ring and tip (red and     บ
 บ  green).  The payphone uses the red and green for its telephone            บ
 บ  operations, but it also uses the yellow and black to control the coin     บ
 บ  mechanism.  Find a section of the wire where a cut will not be easily     บ
 บ  seen.  Strip off the insulation of the cord, exposing the four wires.     บ
 บ  Now, get out the all purpose wire cutters or finger nail clippers if you  บ
 บ  like, and cut the black and yellow wires.  Now just sit back and let      บ
 บ  people use the phone!                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      What Happens?  Well, when you put money into a payphone, it stays in  บ
 บ  the coin mechanism until one of two things happen.  Either you connect    บ
 บ  your call, talk, and hangup; after you hangup, your money goes to the     บ
 บ  collection box.  The only way to get the money then is to rip the box     บ
 บ  out!  Or, you call a number that doesn't answer, or get busy signal, or   บ
 บ  something like that, and then hangup.  When you hangup, the money goes    บ
 บ  from the coin mechanism to the coin return.                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      That is the key!  After the black and yellow wires have been cut,     บ
 บ  the money goes neither to the coin box or coin return!  It just sits      บ
 บ  there!  All you have to do is come back at like 3:00 am in the morning,   บ
 บ  reconnect the black & yellow wires, pick up the handset and put it back   บ
 บ  down.                                                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      All the money that was put in that phone that day comes shooting out  บ
 บ  the coin return, just like in the movies!  It is the COOLEST FEELING!  I  บ
 บ  have collected up to $100 a day doing this to phones all around town!     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      There are some dangers to doing this.  The people that put money in   บ
 บ  and don't get connected or get a busy signal and hang up do NOT get       บ
 บ  their money back.  Usually they will call the operator who in turn calls  บ
 บ  the repair department.  That is why it is important to cut the wire       บ
 บ  where it cannot be seen.  But if you want to do this as a one time        บ
 บ  thing, GO FOR IT!  Oh yes, alternate phones every other couple of days    บ
 บ  or so.  Stay on your toes and watch out for white vans!  If someone sees  บ
 บ  you taking money out of the coin return like getting $15 in change out    บ
 บ  of a phone is not common!  Just say you hung up the phone and all this    บ
 บ  money started pouring out!  It doesn't hurt to give them a little of it   บ
 บ  either!  After a month or two the phone companies catch on, so I do not   บ
 บ  recommend using one phone for over two weeks.                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ    Author  : Trip                                                          บ
 บ    Subject : Salting Coke Machines                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      Salting Soda machines is a fast, easy way of making small amounts of  บ
 บ  money and getting free sodas.  Here are the materials that you will need  บ
 บ  to do it :                                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      1.) Salt (About a big handfull is enough)                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      2.) Some soda (Squirt is best, but Sprite and Coke will work)         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      3.) Something to get the mixture into the soda machine. (I like to    บ
 บ          use a ziplock bag or a balloon.)                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      4.) A soda machine located where nobody is around.                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      First off, you will need to find a soda machine where nobody is       บ
 บ  around.  I use one down at the far corner of my High School because       บ
 บ  nobody ever goes down there.  Now to salt the machine, you will need to   บ
 บ  mix up the Soda (Squirt is best, because it's more acidic) with the salt  บ
 บ  in a plastic ziplock bag, and close it.  Make a hole in one of the        บ
 บ  corners of the bag, (in the opposite end of where the bag closes) and     บ
 บ  shake the bag so the soda and salt mix together.  Now put the end of the  บ
 บ  corner with the hole in it in the dollar bill slot in the soda machine.   บ
 บ  Squeeze the bag so the mixture comes out into the dollar bill slot.  It   บ
 บ  usually takes a 5-10 seconds of squirting it in before you hear a click   บ
 บ  and a whole bunch of quarters come out the coin return.  So now you have  บ
 บ  about 4-5 bucks in quarters.  Well press one of the soda buttons and a    บ
 บ  soda or two should come out.  Now you've got about 5 bucks and a couple   บ
 บ  free sodas.  Damn you could make a living off this shit.                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I recommend covering up your tracks when you are done.  If you made   บ
 บ  an obvious mess, then you should clean it up a little.  You dont have to  บ
 บ  clean the whole fucking machine spotless, but just wipe the salt off.     บ
 บ  This trick is cool because it wont fuck up the soda machine or anything,  บ
 บ  so you can do it as many times as you want.  Have phun.                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ  cool they are?  If you are afraid your group will dump you if you aren`t  บ
 บ  there just get online leave your computer and mark yourself as away how   บ
 บ  hard is that?                                                             บ

 บ  in life.  Computers were made to enhance life not to take it over!        บ

 บ  download all them warez and just chill!  I think the Internet is great    บ
 บ  but it can be destructive because so many people take it too seriously.   บ

 บ  seem as fun.  So also to prolong your enjoyment of the Internet I         บ

 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  06:50 AM - Woke up, dog was rubbing against my leg again.                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  07:10 AM - Finally pushed dog away, it is getting harder to resist those  บ
 บ             "urges."                                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  07:11 AM - Finished morning wrist exercises.                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  07:15 AM - Outta bed.  Time for morning dump.  Don't seem to be able to   บ
 บ             control my ass as well as I used to.  Mental note, stop        บ
 บ             hanging out with Incarnate.                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  07:30 AM - Finally downstairs for breakfast, damn that guy on the         บ
 บ             Wheaties box is sexy.                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  08:00 AM - Log onto AOL (my cool account), I play king of the channel     บ
 บ             for a while.  It is the only place I feel like a man.          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  11:00 AM - 90210 is on!!!  God, Dylan has such an ass!                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  12:00 PM - Log onto IRC.  God, I am soo tired of people laughing at me,   บ
 บ             everything I do turns to shit.  I wonder if I changed my       บ
 บ             name... would that help???  No, some groups have tried it,     บ
 บ             just makes you look lamer.                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  01:00 PM - Lunch time, mommy made me PB&J no crusts, someday I will be    บ
 บ             able to reach the counter top too.                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  02:30 PM - Sailor Moon is on!!!  I know it is gay, BUT I know I will see  บ
 บ             a panty shot in each episode.                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  03:01 PM - Incarnate calls.  We talked about Princess Serena for a        บ
 บ             while.  Then the question I had been dreading, "Do you wanna   บ
 บ             sleep over again tonight?"  I just don't know what to say, my  บ
 บ             ass is still sore from the last time, but I don't wanna seem   บ
 บ             mean.                                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  06:00 PM - Reading book, "How to SCARE the guy who has to go BAD."        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  06:30 PM - W0000 H0000!!!  Big RELEASE!!!!  I just found 2 ppes on a      บ
 บ             local bbs that haven't made it to the Net!!!  I will seem      บ
 บ             like a god to those other release groups!!  2 releases in one  บ
 บ             night!!                                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  07:30 PM - Think I will go outside.  The sun is almost gone, I think it   บ
 บ             is safe.                                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  08:00 PM - Ok Diary, time to pack for Incarnate's house.  Sleeping bag    บ
 บ             for 2, check.  Condoms, check.  Lubrication (won't forget      บ
 บ             that again), check.  Madonna wig, check.  Man, if anyone sees  บ
 บ             this I will be soo embarassed.                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ             might show up for the fun tonight.  I think I can handle it.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  08:50 PM - Spread more untrue rumours about people.  Even if I don't      บ
 บ             know the truth, it is still fun.                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  09:15 PM - Kiss the dog goodbye, at least it doesn't run from me, damn    บ
 บ             women.                                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  09:30 PM - Riding bike to Incarnate's house, someday these training       บ
 บ             wheels will come off!!!  I VOW IT!                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ             life is like.  Good night.                                     บ
