 บ    Author  : Rebel Chicken                                                 บ
 บ    Subject : Lurch Inteviews Me                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      I was about to sleep one night (early morning) when I saw Lurch come  บ
 บ  into channel #RCN.  He starts to interview me, and the following is a     บ
 บ  log of our interview that took place that night.                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 วฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤฤถ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  *** Lurch (xxx@xxxxx.xxx) has joined channel #RCN                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  * Lurch is just scoping out the competition...                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  *** Lurch has left channel #RCN at 12:49AM                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  -Lurch- DCC Chat (10.0.2.15)                                              บ
 บ  *** DCC CHAT (chat) request received from Lurch                           บ
 บ  [E/X] DCC CHAT received from Lurch [xxx@xxxxx.xxx]                        บ
 บ  [E/X] Attempting DCC CHAT with Lurch.                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <RblChickn> What's up?  Long time no chat.                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Lurch> Oh, nothing much man.                                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <RblChickn> Scoping out the competition?  Cool, which e-mag are you       บ
 บ              from?  Can you send over a copy?                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Lurch> Do you want an interview or something?  We're not calling it      บ
 บ          anything new.  We're not making a big deal of it?                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <RblChickn> What is your e-mag going to be called?                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Lurch> Of course I can't send it.                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <RblChickn> Which e-mag did you run again?  Wasn't it called Retro or     บ
 บ              something?  Wait, didn't you guys run Inquisition?            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Lurch> I never ran Retro.  It was lame.  We guys were nothing.  We guys  บ
 บ          are everything.  It is we guys.  Fuck that, it is me guys.        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <RblChickn> What the hell are you babbling?                               บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Lurch> I brought Inquisition to life and it is still me who will keep    บ
 บ          it alive.  You remember me now?                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <RblChickn> Oh yeah...                                                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Lurch> It could be claimed as sad.  For every man in the United States   บ
 บ          know Washington, Jefferson, and Adams.  And yet you do not know   บ
 บ          those which preceeded you.                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <RblChickn> Are you talking about Inquistion preceeding RCN?              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Lurch> Yes.                                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <RblChickn> So Inquisition preceeded RCN?  I guess, I forget, but we      บ
 บ              came from monkeys, so Inquisition is the monkey?              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Lurch> Monkeys is not what we came from.  Monkeys is what we will be.    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <RblChickn> If you say so, you can call yourself a monkey.                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Lurch> From the words of Einstein, "I know not what weapons World War 3  บ
 บ          will be fought with, but I know that World War 4 will be fought   บ
 บ          with sticks and stones."                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <RblChickn> Are you trying to sound smart?  You're not impressing me.     บ
 บ              Do you want me to quote Einstein?  I can do that too,         บ
 บ              "E=mc^2," impressive hey?                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Lurch> It is very unfortunate that you begin to insult, it was the       บ
 บ          wrong move on your part.  You've made the move.  You will get     บ
 บ          the fall.  You will get the fall.  Your pathetically lame e-mag   บ
 บ          which supposedly represents the scene has increased its           บ
 บ          monitored circulation to about 1200 readers.                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <RblChickn> I'm falling outta ma chair, help.. I can't get up.            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Lurch> It is time when the rock of ages falls onto the age of rocks.     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <RblChickn> So how big is Inquisition's "monitored circulation?"  Do you  บ
 บ              still find people reading it now?                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Lurch> I will simply ask you a series of questions.  Weather you reply   บ
 บ          to them, is your choice.  I speak not of Inquisition, which at    บ
 บ          its low had more information than RCN at its high.                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <RblChickn> Woo, a test?  Scary!  Go ahead and ask me some questions.     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Lurch> I don't give tests.  I simply look for a key, a way to see what   บ
 บ          you are, who you are, and weather you are what you claim to be.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <RblChickn> So how big is Inquisition's "monitored circulation?"  I'd     บ
 บ              like to know that information if you're going to say that     บ
 บ              RCN is pathetically lame.                                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Lurch> We are not talking about e-mags, but if you wish to compare,      บ
 บ          Inquisition was read by an average of 4000 scene members, a       บ
 บ          majority of which were a part of the top elite.                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <RblChickn> Well, you're the one bragging about Inquisition.              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Lurch> I did not even mention Inquisition more than twice.  That is not  บ
 บ          the object of my talk with you.                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <RblChickn> Wait, a majority of the 4000 Inquisition readers represent    บ
 บ              the top elite?  A majority is anything over half of the       บ
 บ              whole right?  So 2001 people are part of the top elite?       บ
 บ              This must be a very big scene then.  By the way, weather is   บ
 บ              spelled whether.  I thought I should point that out to you    บ
 บ              since you are an editor of an e-mag.                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Lurch> I know this may sound awkward as a request, but please refrain    บ
 บ          from asking questions at this point.                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <RblChickn> Uhh...                                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Lurch> I am not an editor of an e-mag.                                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <RblChickn> I thought you were the sole person keeping Inquisition        บ
 บ              alive, that's what you said earlier right?                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <Lurch> I should also point out that it is 4 am and I am sitting in       บ
 บ          total darkness and cannot even take responsibility for half the   บ
 บ          shit I type.                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  <RblChickn> Well, you could claim that you are just stupid and not take   บ
 บ              responsibility for what you type.  You don't have to give     บ
 บ              excuses.  So, are you interviewing me?  Or are you just       บ
 บ              going to ask me a series of questions?                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ    Author  : Double O Zero                                                 บ
 บ    Subject : Top 10 Ways to Get Warez                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ
 ษออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออป
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      As we know, being part of the scene means getting free warez.  The    บ
 บ  following are the top 10 ways to get warez :                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  TOP 10 LIST!                                                              บ
 บ  ------------                                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      10.) Put up a board called The Trading Post and put an advertisement  บ
 บ           in your local computer magazine that says, "Free Warez Here!"    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      9.)  Go to your local computer store with a pile of 5ฌ disks and      บ
 บ           start copying software off the display computers.  When they     บ
 บ           tell you that it's illegal say, "Oh, I thought it was            บ
 บ           shareware."                                                      บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      8.)  Get on America Online and join WarezChat.  Say "AN33 N00 W4R3Z,  บ
 บ           d00dZ?"                                                          บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      7.)  Get warez?  Fuck that.  Trade 0 day PORN!                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      6.)  Make sure you know how to type in all the new forms of K-RAD.    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      5.)  Get all COPS (Couriers of Pirated Software) releases.  People    บ
 บ           REALLY want those PhoneDisc installation files.                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      4.)  When you are trading ftp sites, give them 4 random numbers.      บ
 บ           Works every time.                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      3.)  Make sure you know all the good IRC offering channels.  Right    บ
 บ           now, the best one is #0.                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      2.)  Whenever somebody asks you for software say, "I don't have that  บ
 บ           but I have all the releases of SimCity 2000!"                    บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  And the number 1 reason is :                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      1.)  Break out your 300 baud modem and LEECH LEECH LEECH!             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 บ    Author  : Genocide and Loogie                                           บ
 บ    Subject : Top 10 Lamest Things a Release Group Can Do                   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 ศออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออออผ

 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      10.) Have more fixes than actual releases.                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      8.)  DirectX, need I say more?                                        บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      7.)  {Takeover} #Rapesex for personal pleasure, get the pun?          บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ                                                                            บ

 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      3.)  Changing its name more times than it has had working releases.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      2.)  Rip a PCGamer CD-Rom, and calling it a full release.             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  And the number 1 reason is :                                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      1.)  Make a Napalm Guide to Cracking.                                 บ

 บ      RCN is proud to present to the scene the official RCN t-shirt.  We    บ
 บ  tried to keep the price as low as we could so that everyone can enjoy     บ
 บ  these goodies.  Keeping with RCN's volunteerish spirit to help the scene, บ
 บ  Road Rebel has decided to take it upon himself to make the RCN t-shirts   บ
 บ  available to the masses.  This is a non-profit venture and we hope that   บ
 บ  in many ways, RCN continues to benefit the scene.. even when we are not   บ
 บ  near our computers.                                                       บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ       The RCN logo is approximately 8"x6" printed on the back of a        บ
 บ        HEAVY-duty Fruit of the Loom white t-shirt, the front is plain.     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ       A preview of the shirt can viewed upon pressing escape.             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ       Special orders take up to 4 weeks for shipping.                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ  Summary :                                                                 บ
 บ  ---------                                                                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  1.) All RCN issues must be online and available for FREE download.  The   บ
 บ      current issue and back issues must be located in separate file        บ
 บ      directories.  The FULL file_id.diz for the current issue must be      บ
 บ      shown.                                                                บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  2.) A "Reality Check Network" conference must be set up.  The "rcn        บ
 บ      affiliate board" ansi must be shown somewhere in the login process    บ
 บ      or somewhere in the conference join.                                  บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ  3.) Sysops must notify all bulletin board users, via nonconference        บ
 บ      specific mass email, of the new issues available for free download.   บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ                                                                            บ

 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      The new update to the Reality Check Network World Wide Web Site,      บ
 บ  http://www.rcn.org/, adds many new features :                             บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ       Speed Optimization : RCN.org is now speed optimized, which means    บ
 บ        you spend less time waiting and more time browsing.                 บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ       Better Back Issue Access : It's now quick and easy to scan through  บ
 บ        RCN's back issues, each one has its full description online, to     บ
 บ        make searching for the desired issue that much easier.              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ       Better Interface : v2.0 brings an end to the confusing              บ
 บ        conglomeration of pages that previously had existed.  Now speed     บ
 บ        through the icon driven interface to scan back issues of RCN and    บ
 บ        other emags, send comments, read credits, and check out             บ
 บ        merchandise and free files.                                         บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ       Text or JAVA Version : Whatever browser you use can now access the  บ
 บ        RCN.org pages.  Before only Netscape was allowed, but now LYNX and  บ
 บ        other text base users can now access the pages.                     บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ       New Look Graphics : The new graphics style are a nice change of     บ
 บ        pace from the hard-edged style of before.                           บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      To become a file mirror, contact us in #RCN on IRC, you must be able  บ
 บ  to store all back issues in a publically accessible directory from the    บ
 บ  WWW.  A link will be created from RCN.org to your site, so users can      บ
 บ  acquire issues from there if the main site becomes overloaded.            บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      RCN WWW Site       : http://www.rcn.org/                              บ
 บ                                                                            บ
 บ      RCN Mirror Site #1 : http://www.halcyon.com/sbecker                   บ
